‚ÄòKolkata Biriyani‚Äô and Arsalan is a deadly combination. Really misses that when I am not in Kolkata.

Whenever people of KOLKATA talk about Biryani, the name of ARSALAN restaurant comes to mind. It is basically a Mughlai specialty restaurant open since 2002. Biryani is their specialty and one of the most important and famous dish of Mughlai. This RESTAURANT is in the heart of the beautiful city KOLKATA. Close to the market and mall, importantly close to many of the public places. Arsalan have total number of eight outlets in KOLKATA and every outlet is situated in best location of KOLKATA.

In this restaurant we find various "‚ÄôNorth Indian‚Äô, Mughlai & Rolls" cuisines. Here we can find multiple non-veg food items and very few veg food items, all under one roof. Arsalan delivers many flavors in the form of various cuisines of ‚Äú‚ÄôNorth India‚Äô, Mughlai & Rolls.

Arsalan is a Muslim baby name. In Muslim the meaning of the name Arsalan is: Lion (or King of Jungle). According to the name this restaurant gives king feeling to its guest.

Around 11 days ago I visited this place to have dinner with 10 other family members, we all are of different age group. We all ordered multiple starters, dishes and desserts. I can say that it was overall a good and nice experience. 

Their service was not bad, I mean it was good and fast (quick).

Staff of Arsalan is very honest, friendly, courteous, energetic and care full.

I have to admit that each and every food item in starter as well as in main course was properly cooked and their quantity was good as well as sufficient. All of them are tasty and smells very nice. Also each and every dessert item was really fresh and tasty. The texture and presentation of every food item including desserts are simply superb. I love their every food item, it‚Äôs too good

People, 

Ambience was good upto a certain extent, but gives a royalty feeling.

'Cost of Food' is not high. If you want to eat good, hygienic as well as traditional veg and non-veg "‚ÄôNorth Indian‚Äô and Mughlai" food under one roof in good ambience than the cost is good and friendly to the pocket.

Long list of various cuisines in its menu, makes it difficult to decide (because here every dish is yummy and tasty).

I recommend this place to every person of KOLKATA to visit and have food here.

QUALITY OF FOOD: 4/5

QUANTITY OF FOOD: 4.5/5

2017-12-13 11:51:00

5.0
As a biryani lover, i sense biryani to be heaven and tasting biryani from arsalan really fulfils my heavenly wish. Biryani travelled regions it added flavours nd varities. This also added identities to different regions, Motiyon ki biryani from Lucknow, Hyderabadi from Hyderabad, Amritsari from Punjab and many more. Kolkata shares a special relationship with biryani nd arsalan contributes a lot to it.

PHIRNI-Sometimes i get surprised thinking how arsalans managed to make such highly thick, rich nd delicious Phirnis. Its origin from Persia nd now nearly travelled all over the world, its really a mouthwatering dish for the Indians. Known in different regions as payesh, gil-e-firdaus it gained a lot a fame. It is typically served as a desserts. I thnk everyone for once should taste phirnis from arsalan.

Located near the AJC Bose flyover, this is a small branch compared to others. They have two floors though. The interiors were cosy, but it was extremely dark. There was hardly any light for clicking pictures.

Coming to food. The pan fried momos were tough. The filling appeared to be stale. It was a wrong choice to order it.

The chicken tandoori was delicious. It was soft and juicy. It had a fresh taste unlike the momo.

Mutton boti kababs were extremely small. It was soft, but the marination was nothing great. It was okay. It did not bring out the feeling of moghlai food.

The fish tikka kabab was nice. Juicy tender fish cubes, spiced and cooked to perfection.

Butter nan was soft and big.

Chicken Reshmi butter masala was again very tasty. White gravy, cooked to perfection. The chicken pieces were big in size. It was delicately spiced, and the after taste was great.

Coming to the star of Moghlai food the biryani. The mutton piece was tender. The potato was soft and flavourful. The rice grains were long and spiced well. The biryani is a must here.

##

2017-10-25 01:16:16
Pradip Kar
47413057
1.5
This is for all biryani lovers of Kolkata whose mouth starts watering at the slightest mention of the name Arsalan. It has been the same for me as well. Since its inception it has done wonders to our taste buds and now after around fifteen years Kolkatans are crazy for this mughlai dish prepared by the hallowed chefs of Arsalan. Arsalan was like a dream come true for all biryani lovers.

Yesterday was the day when this sweet dream was rudely destroyed by Arsalan of 28, Circus Avenue. I completed some urgent official work and visited Arsalan with all sweet memories that I had gathered for the last fifteen years alongwith my family. Well, mutton kakori kabab, was the one I was dreaming off along with some main course. The waiter straightaway told me that kakori kabab won't be available and have to select some thing from the chicken menu or one or two mutton menu. As Arsalan is not famous for kababs I did not bother and had some basic main course menu like Chicken achari butter masala and roti along with mutton boti kabab. My idea was to savour the biryani luxury at home and ordered for special mutton biryani and normal mutton biryani. The prices were a bit on the higher side but all good things must have some price and so I carried them home. Dinner time I received a biryani shock of my life. The biryani that I got from Arsalan was much similar to the ones served on the roadside for a paltry sum. Though the rice was a bit standard the rudest shock came in the form of mutton. The size has nearly halved compared even to a year back and the soft succulent mutton pieces of yore has become a folk lore and in its stead hard and small mutton pieces could be found inside the rice. Even the chicken egg has come down to koel egg size.

Really, it was like attending the funeral of a dear one who was very much closest to the heart. I would be definitely eating in Arsalan in future as well but the blind faith has taken a backseat now and I would be more cynical in my approach --- not expecting the best or even a good standard biryani offering from them.

Hope this review may have a little effect on the management of Arsalan.

Biriyani King of the town

Any food enthusiast‚Äôs diary in Kolkata is not complete if there is no mention of Arsalan. So here is the review of my favourite Biriyani joint in Kolkata.
This outlet of Arsalan is the closest to its main branch and is located at the starting of the AJC Bose road flyover near Park Circus crossing. We ordered an Arsalan Special Biriyani, a masala Kulcha and a Murg Makhani. The biriyani was as usual not rich and non-oily and tasted heavenly. The masala kulcha was stuffed and filling while the murg makhana had big chunks of chicken and the taste was awesome. However, the chickens seemed a little hard though. The service was okayish and the serving time can be reduced a bit.
Cash and card was accepted. Parking is available in front of the restaurant, under the flyover. 
Definitely recommended.

2017-07-15 15:22:39
Arpita Chattopaddhyay
41293056
5.0
Being a Biriyani Monster, Arsalan is heaven for me...
It never happened that I passed from park circus area  without visiting Arsalan...
It has two areas, Non-Ac and Ac...the non-ac area is a open space with tables and chairs and big fans here and there...nothing special about it's interior or ambience...The AC area is upstairs and the ambience is perfect to taste the heavenly Mughal delicacies...Blue toned lighting, cold and soothing ambience, nicely arranged tables etc..

I haven't found the stuff friendlier than this Arsalan outlet anywhere..They treats us like their children and addresses us with "Beta"...It gives a homely feeling...I don't know they treat every customer like this or only the frequent visitors like me..And most importantly, the stuff give the best suggestion on the dishes we should order...I really love their behavior and hospitality...
Now coming to the food, well if you are a avid biriyani lover like me, Arsalan is the best place to head to...They serve many options in biriyani but I prefer the mutton special biriyani for 2 people most of the time ..they serve the most mouth watering kababs and side dishes...I love the sweet dishes as well...and don't forget to try the oh so good mutton/chicken Halim in the season of Eid... it's authentic and delicious!!
Overall, Arsalan is a zone for foodies and people who love Mughal cuisine...

##

2017-05-05 21:48:56
Sayantan Paul
34840508
4.5
I have been to this place a couple of times for dine in with friends and have parceled food for home a numerous amount of time. Recent visit 15/04/2017. Arsalan especially the branch at park circus one is the best till now in Kolkata. I have been to other outlets but this outlet has its own authenticity. The biryani whether chicken or mutton is the best in the town. The chicken and mutton is cooked so perfectly and is so tender that your taste buds will keep asking for more and more and more.

Food and presentation- First talking about the food it is just-just-just amazing I'll rate it 4.5 out 5. I would deduct 0.5 because I found the oil in the matar paneer was a bit high. Yes, we took one Matar paneer and one of my friends is vegetarian. Chicken biryani requires no description once you grab it will just pamper your taste buds and you will keep having it until it's finished. Kebabs are delicious. Chicken melts in the mouth like Sandesh. Talking about presentation it's pretty simple no extravagant like some 5-star restaurant. Simple and clean white plates for biryani and served with lots of love. For parceled food, the quality is the same as they serve. Big chicken pieces in biryani and the amount they serve is pretty much good enough to fill your tummy.

Ambiance- lovely ambiance. They have two stories. The upper one is AC and the lower one is NON AC. If you are here for food you won't care about AC and NON AC. The decor of the restaurant is pretty good.

Customer service- One of the best in town. Warm welcome. You get a table ASAP if you are not here on a rush day. On the rush day, you would have to line up just like you lined up in banks during demonetization?. No extra charges on festivals or so. Taxes are 20.5% in total. The staff is friendly and good. Washrooms are well maintained. And if you parcel food they provide you with the strongest containers in the market.

Value for money- we were three people and our was merely 800/- INR so yeah pretty cheap. We had a lot of food. Definitely value for money and a must visit for every foodie.

Definitely recommended. Have a good time.

2017-04-06 18:19:29
Roma Chatterjee
32266069
4.5
Hands down, they have the best rolls in Kolkata. You can get me any kind of roll from any place in Kolkata but Arsalan‚Äôs would still be the best for me. I crave for those rolls here because Delhi doesn‚Äôt offer anything like that. You cannot get that taste here at that superbly pocket-friendly price. 

The place offers North Indian and Mughlai cuisines and it‚Äôs known for biryani and tandoor. Zomato shows price for two as Rs. 700 but it has been cheaper for me and fulfilling too. 

My favourite/most eaten item from their menu is the chicken roll. They make the rolls at the front counter so you can see how they go about the whole thing. I don‚Äôt know how it‚Äôs possible but the cooks keep changing from time to time and the taste of these rolls remain the same. There‚Äôs definitely some sorcery behind the making of these rolls. The paratha is always crispy and delicious. The chicken, the julienned onions and sauces do the rest of the magic. I‚Äôve had this roll for breakfast, for lunch and also for dinner. Over the span of 3 years, I have absolutely no count of how many of these I have gobbled down. And all this for just Rs. 45. They say Kolkata has good and cheap food? They‚Äôre right! If you‚Äôre a bit hungrier, just order the double chicken roll (Rs. 65) and I can bet you‚Äôd have not seen so much chicken in a roll before. It‚Äôs very filling. Stuff like that just makes your smile broader. Get an egg chicken roll and you‚Äôll probably get wings (not chicken wings!). The paneer roll is also good but obviously I prefer chicken. I‚Äôve had rolls from a lot of places in Kolkata, a lot of famous places, but Arsalan stands unmatched.¬†
Obviously, Arsalan doesn‚Äôt just offer rolls. That‚Äôs like their cheapest flagship product. Get deeper into their menu and you‚Äôll see other mouth-watering delicacies.

Their kebabs are finger lickin‚Äô good. I‚Äôll recommend all of them because I‚Äôve had most of them and I‚Äôve never been disappointed. Kebabs are love. Their chicken malai kebab is succulent and creamy (I‚Äôve always been fond of chicken malai kebabs but theirs is simply impressive). The best on their list is the chicken tengri kebab. You can never go wrong with this choice. It‚Äôs spicy, a great, balanced combination of all the flavours and they give you a good quantity even if it‚Äôs just 2 pieces. They are some big, juicy chicken legs; sexy af. All the kebabs are cooked in a tandoor.

There is one kebab whose name I haven‚Äôt seen on the menu ever but have eaten at the Park Street outlet. It‚Äôs called Arsalan special kebab. It‚Äôs basically pieces of meat marinated in spices, grilled on skewers and has a thick layer of cheese on it. Almost like seekh kebab but bigger and better. It‚Äôs even better than the tengri kebab. The cheese does all the magic. It is a must have. All kebabs are served with onion juliennes, lemon and green chutney, which is also A plus; it‚Äôs mixed with curd and, hence, is not that spicy which is perfect for me. 

Arsalan is famous for its biryani. Well, Kolkata is famous for biryani. I‚Äôve had chicken biryani from Arsalan, that too only once because I‚Äôm not very fond of biryani. Personally, I believe biryani is bit overhyped (a lot of bad words coming my way?). Yes, it‚Äôs convenient to eat but I prefer rice and chicken curry. Some people just serve bland and tasteless biryani and beam with pride over other people‚Äôs fake compliments. I keep mum. I‚Äôd rather stay shut than do false praising. Arsalan‚Äôs biryani was, thus, okay for me (get a cold drink with it though). I think, people in my family make more flavoursome biryani. 

¬†The mutton pasinda (shredded mutton in gravy) is good. It‚Äôs one of my uncle‚Äôs favourite. He orders it every time. My favourite gravy items are chicken boneless masala and kadhai murgh. These paired with their butter naan is just the best lunch you can have. Truly. The boneless masala has a hot gravy and they use kebabs for the chicken pieces which I think makes all the difference. You get a chicken gravy item plus kebabs with great texture. The kadhai murgh has North Indian flavours and is loaded with veggies. When everyone else is eating biryani, this is what you should order (I did that :P). Also, chicken butter masala is good. Chicken bharta (shredded) has a lot of oil floating on top but if you can put that aside it is a good choice for those who don‚Äôt like spicy food much (appropriate for kids I suppose). Chicken Kashmiri was a bit sweet (I need emojis here). To be honest, I‚Äôm checking out their menu simultaneously and all of the chicken in gravy items are good: chicken reshmi butter masala, chicken tengri, murgh makhani and I‚Äôve mentioned so many already. Just order whatever and it‚Äôll be good, even the vegetarian dishes (except for paneer kofta; it was weird and sweet). Wasn‚Äôt all this so mouth-watering? I‚Äôm hungry (chicken masala and butter naan <3). I have to go to Kolkata soon.

I think they have a slight inclination towards adding some sweet flavour in some of the dishes. Slight. It‚Äôs probably a Mughlai cuisine thing but I did not know it back then. Like, for example, I was trying to experiment once and, so, I ordered the Arsalan special naan. It costed 80 bucks and, ergo, I had high expectations. I had ordered some gravy dish too to go along with it. Much to my horror, it was sweet. I had thought that it would be loaded with spices, butter/cheese or contain chicken keema maybe. I definitely did not expect the special naan to be sweet. That was just one weird experience.

2017-02-13 12:30:59
Shahrukh Ahmed
15540184
4.0
The Bengalis and Kolkataians in particular, delights themselves even with the term Biryani. Although, I myself am a 'Biryani Boy', I have no such fascination owing to a reason that it is prepared on a regular basis at my household. However, I am bound to have biryani in a restaurant just because my friends are universally biryani freak.

When it comes to having this "Spicy Rice with Meat", Arsalan was the the ultimate choice among many, which with passage of time has gradually declined. However, my encounter with this restaurant was okaish. On more than couple of occasion, during the past few years, I have been to Arsalan and tried just Biryani with occasional sides in the name of Soft Drinks, Firni and Salad. I have had tasted in both the outlets of Park Circus, but, I tend to prefer Circus Avenue over 7 Point, may be because of the less crowd in the former one over latter.

Although this outlet is smaller one, I have had experienced less people approaching it, most probably because of the locational difficulties. However, the taste of food in both these outlets seems identical and it denotes that the food is cooked in one kitchen itself. The staff are okay behaved but the services are slow, comparatively.

Irrespective of the outlets visited, I have seen a gradual decrease in taste of Arsalan over the years which has considerably reduced my visits to the place. But, I can successfully conclude that it still serves tastier and quality biryani than many outlets in the city.

2017-02-09 09:39:13
Raja Mukherjee( SpiceRoot2Gastronomy)
37606952
3.0
My biggest weakness is Lucknow nababi cuisine and Moghulai food.

Arsalan is one choice which has evolved over the last decade defacing competitors Aminia,Shabir,Rahmania,Biryani Hut to name a few.

My biggest problem with these eateries are that they all have evolved into GenX eateries with great facilities but their kitchens are yet to.

It is equally important that  cooks, stewards and cleaning sections evolved to the requirements of food safety and cleanliness in today's perspective when human life is threatned with unknown virus 
and bacteria attacks.

While eating in many of Arsalan joints I have found the utensils clean but to my doubt not fully santised.

The hygiene class of the kitchen and their cooks,are two most important and basic factors which I shall take into considerations while taking out friends and family out to an eatery.

 Cleanliness and sanitisation of plates,forks and spoons are equally important while considering a good palate.

Arsalan's special Mutton kababs and biryani are one of the best and I prefer take aways over sitting and eating.The place is too crowded and the quick serving and eating bothers me a lot. I always prefer to unwind myself with friends and relatives and relax a bit while eating out.

Management can implement steam based vaccum cleaning systems to help customers enjoy safe and healthy food.

2017-01-29 00:53:41
Ankur Chakraborty
434085
2.5
Arsalan is another iconic place I had heard so much about. Being a non-resident Bengali, never had the opportunity to try this place; and being a die-hard biriyani lover, always had a wish to go here someday.

Visited this place for dinner on 25th December evening. Waiting time was reasonable, and we were ushered to the first floor once table was available.

The seat we were offered had an AC unit overhead, and it was leaking. And not drop by drop but some heavy constant leakage. We asked for a different seat, and the waiter told us pretty rudely that this is the only place left and either we had to take it or leave it. After some argument, the manager intervened and assigned a different table reluctantly. -0.5 for such rude and unprofessional behaviour.

We ordered mutton tikka and mutton biriyani. Tikka was kind of burnt, and the mutton was really really hard. The biriyani was good, but I did not find anything to justify the "iconic" tag. I had had same standard of Kolkata-style biriyani in Mumbai, Hyderabad and Bangalore too. -1 for not-so-good food.

Service was very slow and pathetic. We ordered one cold drink at the time of ordering and it came after we had almost finished the meal, and after multiple reminders. -1 for the service too.

Oberall, IMHO, neither I could find anything that justifies the "iconic" tag, nor I would be too willing to go back there.

2016-12-18 20:48:51
Dru_monk
32567471
4.5
Ever heard of chota packet, bada dhamaka! This place truly depicts this saying. I had heard a lot about arsalan's food from my friends and also read about it on zomato. When you see it from outside, it looks like some regular small restaurant but when it comes to food, it is mind boggling.

Me and my friends went for lunch. We ordered one mutton biryani, two special chicken biryani, one chicken chap, one kadhai chicken and one assorted kebab platter.

The biryanis were delicious. In Kolkata, biryanis have both meat and potato. This was something I had never heard of. The quantity was more than sufficient and the taste was superb. I Loved it.

The kadhai chicken was dead spicy and made the biryani taste better. The gravy was so tasty that we requested for extra gravy. I didn't like the chap much. It was too oily and was kind of bland in front of other dishes.

The assorted kebab platter had chicken, fish and lamb kebabs. The chicken and fish kebabs were amazing. I didn't like the lamb kebabs much.

Overall, a very reasonable place with a lot of offering. A must try for all the biryani lovers.

##

2016-10-11 23:45:07
Dr. Shrayan Pal
35467501
3.5
Review: Arsalan Restaurant, Park Circus

Location - 5/5
At exactly Park Circus 7 point crossing no one will have difficulty finding it, even if they don't have any help from google map. Reachable by surface public transport from any part of Kolkata very easily.

Facilities - 2.5/5
No parking facilities from the hotel, parking nearby is a tad bit difficult, specially in festive times and weekends. You can pack your food and there is a separate counter for that outside, and they don't take too long for that.

Ambiance - 2.5/5
Clearly not for the guys who expect a very nice ambiance, and somehow everything around the place screams "cheap", not to mention the overcrowding of tables. But it is clean and not very uncomfortable in matter of table heights & seating arrangements.

Food - 4/5
For Biriyani and most kababs-rezalas-chaaps kind of foods one of the best places at Kolkata. But, the food type is tilted more towards Mughlai, rather than Hyadrabaadi cooking style, but modified well to suit bengali palate. Food during festive seasons are bit off compared to normal days. Pricing will feel value for money for most items.

Service - 3.5/5
Not very polished, but not crude either. If you don't care much about sophistication, warm courteous service only does well for you, then not a bad place to be. And, naturally when pressure is too high, during weekends and festive seasons, service quality falls a bit.

Overall - 3.5/5
Not a bad place if only thing matters to you is food, and not the total ambiance and all.

Recommendations:¬†

For when, writing a review for Park Circus Arsalan is just a trivial matter as everybody has got their own notion about it.
Standing tall amidst the 7-point crossing of Park circus, this place literally exudes the flavoursome smell of Mughlai all around. Well the lower portion is mainly non-ac and the 1st floor is AC with dim lights and well furnished decor having the perfect dining ambience.
Tried quite a few different items in each of my visits.
‚Ä¢ Chicken Biryani : A plate full of long grained basmati biryani with a humongous piece of chicken and potato. I don't prefer awadhi biryani much as because they don't serve ALU with it, being a Bengali it's tough to gulp biryani without ALU. Without going into superfluous description about this dish I can put it as the "BEST BIRYANI IN KOLKATA".
‚Ä¢ Chicken Tengri Kebab : this meat kabab is my personal favourite, chicken leg pieces well marinated with spices and well roasted and then assorted with salads and a super tasty Dhaniya-curd chutney.
‚Ä¢ Mutton Boti Kebab : moderate pieces of mutton roasted in a stick with veggies and served in a platter with pudina-curd chutney.
‚Ä¢ Chicken Chap : another favourite of all time, as well a arsalan speciality.
‚Ä¢ Shahi Tukhra : An extravagant sweet dish made up in form of bread pudding with kesar n dry fruits kheer can blast someone's taste buds.
.
Here staffs are well-behaved and prompt as well, although the place gets crowded with time and then service gets slow.
.
Pocket pinch is moderate with taxes.
.
RATINGS : ;
FOOD : 4.5/5
AMBIENCE : 4/5
SERVICE : 3.5/5
VFM : 4.5/5
.
HIGHLY RECOMMENDED!

2016-08-13 16:35:48
Dibya Jit
14541441
4.5
There are two restaurants of Arsalan at Park Circus Area. One is at the 7 point crossing while the other is at Beck Bagan. To me,  the second outlet is somewhat better than the first one. Though,  my personal favourite in terms of service is the branch at Park Street.

Why Arsalan?
If you love Biryani and if you want to taste of the greatest biryanis in town, you have to be here.

What to have?
Ofcourse biryani! Beside that,  you can start off with a plate of Malai Kebab and take a side dish like chicken chap or mutton rezala,  though it is not mandatory.
End up with firni or shahi tukda.

Pocket Pinch?
Reasonable and worthy,  as you are paying for one of the best Mughlai foods of the town.

Service?
As I mentioned earlier,  Park Street Branch tops the list. Then comes the Beck Bagan branch which is at a walkable distance from the 7 point crossing branch.
You might have to wait to get a seat at the 7 point crossing branch. I am yet to visit the Ruby branch.
Hati Bagan branch is also good.

##

2016-08-13 13:31:05
Debanjan Banerjee
35593948
4.5
Food: For all kolkata biriyani lovers , this is heaven. Biriyani is full of flavor , rice quality is excellent , Mutton is well coocked, if you are unlucky sometime mutton can be medium cooked. Mutton stew goes well with mutton biriyani, its spicy and awesome. Arsalan special kabab is also good.

Service: The only issue with the old park circus outlet is you have to wait to get a table. There is another outlet in park circus which is better (service wise) . Park street outlet is also spacious, best is the new outlet in ruby. 

Ambience: Arsalan is all about food , not ambience. Newer outlets in Ruby has an excellent ambience as well.

Known For : Mutton biriyani, Chiken Biriyani, Kababs, Mutton chap, Chicken Chap, Mutton Stew.

If you are hungry, Craving for Biriyani, This Is The Place.

2016-07-31 09:07:19
Debjit Basu
31827922
4.5
Been there with my father and sister some time ago. Everyone knows that arsalan is the king of biriyani so we decided to try it out. When we entered the restaurant it was almost vacant. The dining space was a bit small but the seats were well arranged making adequate space for dining
The ambience was decent and the staff attended us well. Nowpving on to the dishes

1. Chicken reshmi kabab - the star of the day. It just outsurpassed our expectations. Tender pieces of chicken shimmered in reshmi gravy
 A hit. The dish was served us hot and quickly. I would give it 4.8.

2. Chicken tikka kabab - not as great as the reshmi kabab. But yet one decent dish. Chicken pieces cooked in spicy Indian gravy. The taste was quite decent. A 4.2.

3. Chicken biriyani - we came here to taste the biriyani and as all say it was heavenly. The chicken pieces were tender and quite big. Not overfilled with spices and oil. Altogether a great dish. A 4.5.

4. Chicken tikka butter masala   - my favourite dish and it was also really great. Tender juicy chicken pieces cooked in spicy tikka gravy with cream and butter. Heavenly isn' t it. I would give it a 4.4.

5. Mutton biriyani - another star dish of the day. Arsalan was frankly the first place where I tasted any mutton preparation and it was worth it. The mutton pieces were greatly cooked and level of spices was balanced
Indeed a great dish. A 4.5

6. Firni - the firni is a dessert one can have in Muslim restaurants. It was really a great dish and it ended our dining greatly. A 4.5.

The bill was reasonable and I would surely revisit this place.

But the taste was good and it was light. The tandoori chicken was the best part of our meal. The portion was good and the chicken itself was flavourful. But I'm not a fan of their mutton chaap, usually the mutton pieces are too tough and rubbery. The gravy was good though. But these minor issues somehow made my meal a little unsatisfactory. But anyway, it disappoints less. But the place is pocket-friendly and always busy. So the food served is always fresh and even the portions are decent compared to the price tags.

2016-07-06 08:02:51
Pallab Mukherjee
31907103
4.5
I have visited this restaurant at least fifty times but never got a chance to post a review, so finally decided to write one. This is based on my experience last week, so it is all fresh.¬†

Lets talk about the food first. If you are a fan of North Indian food, Biriyani, kebabs then Arsalan is a must try for you. ¬†Chiken Tandoori is delicious, juicy and hot. If you are a vegetarian, try Crispy chilli baby corn or chilli potato. They are not famous for Chinese dishes, but you will be amazed to see the quality.¬†

For the main course, after trying several items, this is what I will recommend. Go for Garlic Naan, Biriyani and Chicken Tikka Butter Masala. Biriyani is one of the best in Kolkata and you already know that. I have tried many different types of Naan here and that includes Kabuli and Keema naan. But the garlic naan is undoubtedly the best. For the chicken items, Chiken Lahori I have ¬†tried before but I didnt like it that much. Chicken Tikka butter masala contains 6 large pieces of chicken in a very rich, thick gravy. Lovely. If you are fussy about oil content, then this dish is not for you.¬†

Staff are good. However, they are busy. You dont expect extra attention like what you get in some other restaurants.¬†

Ambience is good too. Now they have built a floor at the top, so you can enjoy comfortable sofa. Also, this floor is spacious.¬†

Price - it is cheap. You cant get a better bargain at that quality and quantity.¬†

I recommend.

A Halt For Haleem

Whenever I think of any mughal delicacies, the first name flashes in my mind is Arsalaan. I don't know why I have such an affection towards this restaurant but definitely it never ever disappointed me.

Last Saturday I went to this newer branch of arsalaan, beside the A.J.C Bose road fly over especially for haleem. I think this part of arsalaan is mainly for taking away or delivery because while getting to the table we were asked thrice whether we want delivery or not. The interior is most like the upstairs of the main arsalaan at park circus 7 points. We ordered mutton haleem, rumali roti and green salad. The taste was haleem was too good. Just like what I thought of ! It was neither spicy, nor oily and not at all heavy. The tiny pieces of mutton were soft and submerged in the thick gravy of haleem. One plate of haleem is sufficient for two people. I don't have any complain about the quality but yes, the green salad should more decorated when served. I saw this joint is also have chinese items in the menu. I will be there soon to have a glimpse of that :)

##

2016-03-27 16:04:50
Shreya Chakraborty/tinkering_tastebuds
4607741
4.5
This place needs no introduction perhaps. Although Arsalan has opened its branches all over Kolkata, with Park Circus itself housing two of them, this is perhaps the most popular one. And with the recent addition of the second floor, its room for accommodation has gone up. It's one of the oldest biriyani houses in the city, and people who have tasted their biriyani can hardly find a better one. However, apart from the Biriyani, which is quite spicy and undoubtedly delicious, my other favourites from this place are the Arsalan Special Chicken Cheese Kabab, and their Phirni.

Now, you can order any kabab you want, and be assured that it's cooked in the perfect Mughlai style, with the right amount of apices. But the Cheese Kabab is, hands down, their best. The cheese just melts in your mouth, and with the chutney, the taste is out of the world. The chicken or mutton side dishes are equally good, with the Chicken Reshmi Butter Masala being one of my all-time favourites from the place. And to end it all, the Phirni. Try it to get the real taste of it. Mere words cannot describe it.

You're not a true Mughlai lover, if you've not visited this place. Highly recommended!

4.0
This is the only Arsalan outlet I come to, whenever I plan of having Biryani. Also, while my stay in Mumbai, I had always missed the Biryani out here. So, while am in Kolkata and Biryani is on my list for lunch or dinner, this outlet of Arsalan is my favourite. I have come here may be innumerable number of times, most of the times with my elder brother and sometimes alone. You basically dont need a company out here, all you concentrate here is the food. Inspite of my several number of visits out here, this is the first time am writing a review and am happy about it that for the first time am reviewing my favorite Biryani joint on Zomato.
Location wise its the easiest to find, tell any cab driver to take you to Park Circus Arsalan, he will take you but yes, please do mention that Bridge ke niche wala Arsalan and not the Seven point one. 
The number of times I have visited this place, I have always found this place full of people. I most of the times get the same table to sit, coincidentally. Being a regular customer, the waiters and managers are very well acquainted with me and they always treat their customers with much respect and value thats what I live about this outlet. I have become so regular out here that the waiters doesnot even give me the menu now whenever I visit, because even they have to come to know what I will be ordering. Haha! Most of the times, I order Chicken Biryani, sometimes I change it for Mutton Biryani when am
High on my red meat cravings, a sweet lime drink is a must for me, and to end my meal with a dessert, I go for their special Firni which is another delicacy I love from them. Sometimes, I go for Chicken Tandoori when I accidentally become little diet conscious. üòÉ
Biryani - the aroma of Arsalan, finely selected rice, the aloo that they add in it, the juicy tender chicken/mutton pieces, the spices, the tenderness and taste everything adds up to make it a delicacy worth eating from time to time, everytime. I just love it! Coming to the tandoori, they serve it well-grilled, with very little oil used, non-greasy, well spiced-up, with a good quantity of salad of cucumber and onions finely chopped in round pieces, and the yummy raita of dahi and finely chopped onions. Sweet lime that they serve is so refreshing, that I order it the first before I start off with my main course. I love their Firni and I never miss out on it, it just has the perfecr taste with the perfect amount of sweetness and milkiness, the rice granules are so fine that you can actually feel the softness, they are served chilled and with a kesar flavor which you can make out from the aroma of the dessert.
The prices are always pocket-friendly. Sometimes, when I go for a take-away order, my bills are exempted of the service taxes also, only the mrp (inclusive of taxes) mentioned on the menu are added up. I love this Arsalan outlet and will keep visiting it time and again. ‚úåüèªÔ∏èüòä

2016-01-22 11:13:19

4.0
If you are in Kolkata and haven't tried Arsalan for some Biryani and kebabs then you have missed out the most popular and yummy biryani in the city .
Located in park circus 7 point crossing this restaurant is running the business for years now and till date they have expanded their business over the city remarkably capturing foodie lovers to dwell in their food experience . Arsalan has two seating arrangement so they had made two floor where one will have air condition which is on top and the ground will be without air but sufficient fans to cool you , and restrooms is also there that is kept clean .
Coming to the food I must say they really have some seriously good flavoured biryani sufficient enough for 1 person and in fact little more for one person to eat so they dont compromise with quantity , then the ingredients is very rich which does give you a feel of a high standard biryani making it always a choice on priority for people who love biryani.
Apart from biryani other dishes and foods are available Indian breads like naan , roomali also they have rice there, different types of curries like chicken kassa ,chicken chaap , kebas are all prepared with the same standard for years now.
Moving over heavy meal now Arsalan also has roll counters outside the restaurant as you enter you will spot it making rolls for people to just have a quick bite which is made very nice and garnished well too.
With everything seem to be close to perfect over here I always feel the price factor at times is a look out but nevertheless food is simply ( A ) standard and I tend to come here on a regular note .

Cook Must have forgotten salt & added more garam masala instead. I added raw salt & had. Well, 2nd day at my friends house at Diamond City. They picked up from Park Circus crossing one. It was ok.

3rd Time I picked up from Circus Avn on the last monday of december & again it was so 'Teekha'. I never heard or had Awadhi Biryani so spicy hot - not even from Arsalan. It had always been a mild spicy & sweeter in taste as the mutton they cook marinated with Khowa / Malai.

Dear Arsalan, I know, your name is growing faster than usual, going far places in moments -- but Pls dont go so far that its gonna be tough to retufn

##

2015-12-29 17:30:09
Somnath Chattopadhyay
29211665
4.0
No doubt Arsalan is one of the prime leaders in Biryani at Kolkata. I have started my journey with Arsalan around 10-11 years back. At that time, it was only one, the main 7 point crossing restaurant. Now they have come up with many branches, but I still prefer the 7 point crossing old and main joint.¬†

Arsalan Biryani has it's distinct signature with a kind of well balanced juicy texture. It's not that oily, but it is rightfully done to preserve it's moisture. The nose and palate both feels excellent distinctive character. The note of ghee is slightly less dominating compared to Shiraz. But very well balanced. I noticed the Garam Masala, to be specific cinnamon is slightly more dominating over kewda or rose water. Saffron gives a right aroma and colour, while the mutton fat adds a perfect savory flavor. There are two versions of mutton biryani there, the ordinary and special. I always go for the special one, not because there are two pieces of mutton, but I always found some dried fruits in the biryani, which adds up more flavor.¬†

Generally I do not go for Chicken biryani, because I do not identify Chicken biryani with my taste. Along with the biryani, I always like to have a green salad and nothing else. Not even any cold drink. To me, mixing any other flavor with Biryani is a serious offense.¬†

The service at the busy hours can be frustrating. But that goes with the fem of every restaurant in the city. You attract more with your good quality and ¬†your service suffers. Thankfully, it is only the quality service that suffers with the huge crowd not the quality of the food.¬†

I am a big fan of Arsalan. But I have one advice to the people who are going to taste Arsalan Biryani for the first time. Have it there itself. Don't take it to your home. The magic disappears with time.¬†

For the Kababs, all are good. They have a special Arsalan kabab, which is kind of Chiken reshmi wrapped with cheese and then baked. But somehow, I think this doesn't go with the Mughlai tradition of the restaurant. They should change the name of the dish, as Arsalan is known for Mughlai cuisine, and this dish is a fusion dish.

2015-12-02 22:04:40
RGupta
32642663
1.0
At the time of writing, this place has a rating of 4.3 with 3311 votes. I apologise if I hurt your foodie sentiments, but based on my today's dinner experience at Arsalan Park Circus, I rate it as an overhyped, overgrown, rotten, dingy, filthy place to taste good Biriyani at Kolkata. Again, based on my sole experience, I vehemently oppose all the good ratings and reviews this place has received so far. Either the Kolkata Biriyani lovers have completely lost it, or there is a problem with the review system, or most of the reviews are posted by the near and dear ones of the restaurant's owners, or I was plain unlucky, or a mix and match of some or all of these. Here is why:

1. The ambiance: Old, filthy and dirty. The floors are "divided by two". No fans, only split ACs right above the tables. Nice way to stay cool! Tiny tables meant for 2 had 3 chairs, when we requested for 2 chairs only, the waiter needed to seek an approval from the higher management if that could be done. The city and red tapes - inseparable.

2. The waiters: Clueless of which is which. We ordered Arsalan special Biriyani. We wanted the authentic Arsalan Mutton Biriyani, and that was the one suggested by the waiter. Here is where the problem started. What we received was RED SPICY RICE with no flavor. When we enquired what was it supposed to be, the supervisor said it is South Indian Biriyani. South what? We came all over to have the South Indian Biriyani which is from Kolkata? Flawless! It had 2 mutton pieces which were hidden in the red rice, if you know what I mean. Bravo.

3. The management: Further to that, I went downstairs and complained to the people at the cash counter downstairs, it had 2 senior people, and while I mentioned that problem of how come your authentic Biriyani was missing the a of authenticity, he turned it around and had the audacity to blame us for wrong ordering - "aap ko pata hona chahiye tha aap kya order kar rahe ho". Yeah of course Sir, I should have known your version of special Biriyani is nothing but spicy red rice. Bravo. He offered me a consolation prize of a complimentary pack of mutton Biriyani which I now taste as no better.

All in all, my personal opinion is, Arsalan Park Circus has grown too big for its shoes and has forgotten usual stuff like ambiance, customer service and of course food quality. I will of course never venture near, nor would recommend. Go there at your own risk. PS: It does not provide good photo ops too, only you may post an update saying that you have been there, or maybe you will be more social if you broadcast you had been there or say you live for and like the food there. Good luck! Aminia, Shiraz, Zeeshan, Alibaba, here I come.

##

2015-11-30 21:28:08
Bedanta Chakraborty
29654006
4.5
Arsalan is an evergreen restaurant which never seems to run out of fashion.
Whenever I am in town I make a point to visit this place. It has been probably 10 years I am eating in this place and yet I still cherish Arsalan.
MUTTON BIRIYANI in Arsalan is always an obligatory choice. For me it's as if Mutton Biriyani is the deity in the Mecca of Arsalan. With succulent and soft and juicy mutton coupled with a dum potato, and the beautifully flavoured Biriyani, Arsalan always manages to tickle my taste buds for good. The main feature of the dish is its ridiculously pleasant and 'Mon bhorejawar' aroma. It's as if the aroma in itself is sufficient to please your tummy. For me Mutton Biriyani in Arsalan is a habit, and a good habit must always be treasured.
FIRNI
A post Biriyani sweet dish, FIRNI in Arsalan is a beautiful pudding and a good appetising dish in Arsalan is never consummated if not for a FIRNI. It has this incisive sweetness, which I absolutely adore. And so, FIRNI in Arsalan is always a welcoming dish for me.
KEBABS
Apart from the brilliant Biriyani they serve, Arsalan is well known for its Kebab. Smokey and tasty as they are, the different kebabs they serve will surely conjure your taste buds for good. The Reshmi Kebab and the Malai kebab are always asked for and hence are pleasured.

Normally, I generally give a lot of importance to service and ambiance. However, for special instances as in this case, one may turn a blind eye towards those aspects for the food they serve is happiness personified. That being said, I absolutely love as to how quick they serve the food and yet they are fresh. I always love the fact that even though the waiters are super busy, they still lend a ear suggesting you different combinations, and I haven't yet encounters any unpleasant behaviour so far. A kudos to the entire Arsalan family.

Bon apetit üëå

2015-11-24 10:27:06
Anuvrat Pabrai
15672792
1.5
Having heard so much about Arsalan, we decided to go there with family last night . We were 6 of us. Being a Monday the restaurant was nearly empty with just 2-3 tables occupied. 

We ordered - 

Chicken Reshmi Kebabs as starters 

Chicken Biryani

Mutton Biryani

Chicken Kashmiri

Mutton Pasinda 

Chicken Bharta 

Roti's

The Chicken Reshmi Kebabs were very dry and tough - a result of just being reheated and served. On complaining , they brought another 2 plates but they were also dry and tough. 

The gravy items served were luke warm and we had to send them for reheating . 

The Biryani- somehow the rice is not fully cooked and the grains are also smaller . Dryish and again not hot . To be fair the Mutton piece was thankfully cooked and soft . 

The rotis were undercooked and cold. 

By this time we had lost the entire appetite to eat . 

What made it worse was that the staff was busy chit chatting with each other and appeared to be discussing us as if we were from Mars and had no business to complain. 

Few well meaning suggestions for Arsalan to improve - 

1. Do spend some effort to train and retrain your serving staff.  

2. Have someone senior to oversee operations . It appears that no one senior was in the establishment and no one appeared in command of the place or  interested to work 

3. Serve food piping hot . 

4. Get a good kebabchi . Your kebabs were an utter disappointment 

5. Train your serving staff to understand that indian food needs to be served with serving staff careful about rotis being served at the correct time and should be piping hot. 

I know Arsalan is a much popular place but to me they just don't seem to be able to get their act together . It would take a lot of persuasion for me  to attempt another visit.

We ordered for mutton biryani and believe me it was awesome with tender and flavourful mutton pieces along with aromatic rice. Too good!! We also asked for chicken reshmi kabab which was also delectable and went well with biryani. All these at fairly decent price.

A must visit for one who have not tried here before and get a taste of this legendary place.

##

2015-08-30 16:53:07
Debajyoti (www.foodiedada.com)
1855976
4.0
I have actually lost count of the number of times I have been to this legendary outlet of Arsalan, but the strangest fact is - I never felt the urge to review it. Because I thought it needs no review, the food at this place speaks for itself. But after ordering from this joint last week my opinions changed a bit and I felt I need to pass on some suggestions and opinions about this landmark outlet. It was an office-delivery order and the total bill was over INR 5000/- and so we expected really good overall experience. Well, we almost reached there barring few points. We were told that orders from Sector-5 will be delivered only if the order value is more that INR 2000/-. We were fine with that point since we had almost 20 people for that lunch meet. But still after delivering, the delivery boys kept on asking for extra tip!

DELIVERY PROCESS: Well we had called them up a day earlier and placed our final order since they said you need to place the order a day ahead if you do not want your food to be delivered late. But then also after accepting the order (a day earlier) they said the food can't be delivered before 1:30 PM. We wanted to go for Arsalan, so we did not cancel the order. Next day we were pleasantly surprised when the food was delivered few minutes before 1PM. But then the delivery boys should stop asking and nagging for extra money, that's really irritating.

FOOD ORDERED: We went in for Chicken Biriyanis, Mutton Biriyanis and few plates of Chicken Tikka Butter Masala. The side dish i.e. the Chicken Tikka Butter Masala had 6 pieces of juicy chicken kebabs per plate in very thick and rich gravy which is extremely tasty, sinful and oily. The Biriyanis also tasted divine, the quality of rice was good and it was overall not so oily. The sweet potato was very well cooked, flavorful and was almost melting in the mouth. But sadly my packet mistakenly had two pieces of large potatoes and hence had very little rice in it which was extremely disappointing. The main concern is ‚Äì The quantity per plate has gone down drastically, we were still hungry after finishing our meal. That was very sad and extremely embarrassing for the organizers. Maybe this is only true for their home/office delivery orders, because I had a much better experience when I used to dine-in here at this joint. The joint has got no ambiance, remains over-crowded and has got mediocre service, but the food quantity served here is always sufficient and ofcourse no questions about the taste. These biriyanis now cost INR 170/- and it is truly disheartening if they still can‚Äôt fill in your tummy. Also I found the mutton piece in the biriyani had huge bones that might have occupied most of the space in that biriyani packet, sadly the mutton in there was not so soft, it was bit chewy and dry, that is so unlike Arsalan! But still I‚Äôll rate the food joint 4 out of 5 because this was not my first meal here, I really had splendid meals here several times in the past.

SUMMARY: Here are my granular ratings for this place:

Food quality: 4.1/5
Food quantity: 3/5
Food presentation: 3.4/5
Food packaging: 3.4/5
Delivery process: 3.6/5
Ambiance: 3.4/5
Value for money: 3.7/5
Service: 3.5/5

Overall this still remains one of my favorite spots to savor some delicious biriyani in the city. Maybe we won‚Äôt be going in for big office-deliveries again, but still we will keep on visiting this place for some memorable dine-in experiences.

Cheers!

For Price sensitive people(like me), If you choose to sit & dine then add Rs. 10/- to each item on the menu card displayed at Zomato website (The menu displayed here at the website is the takeaway menu) and thereafter add 20.1% (5.6% S.Tax + 14.5% VAT) to the total bill to calculate the actual amount that you shall be paying.
Chicken Reshmi Butter Masala & Arsalan Special Kebab ( Cheese Kebab) are sure to steal your heart.
Time & again, the same request if possible, please publish/display your menu card with all inclusive prices.

2015-07-23 16:51:49
Nabankur Paul
11614851
1.5
Pandit Manish Sharma is a very talented musician , who plays Jaltarang so well that , there are times one quivers whether a water fall is nearby , he can also create the same magic by using various utensils and crockeries , one of those instrument is thejal tarang. I always dreamt to play the instrument like him , my visit to Arsalan restaurant in Park circus accidentally created that opportunity for me , it was 17th of July'15 , me and my family made our way up to a dimly lit Air Conditioned enclosure to enjoy a lunch , which resembles more like an underworld infested gambling den than food joint. Tables and chairs are packed in that limited space to accommodate as many foodies they can,such was the comfort that, one can rest his arm on his neighbours shoulder while having the meal. We could somehow locate a table and piled and jostled around each other centering the table. After settling in , we observed in disbelief, that even after spending considerable amount of time , not a single waiter approached our table. Then I located a silent man , possibly the cashier , sitting in the farthest corner of the room with a small pile of table mat kept on the table in front of him. I could attract his attention and requested for a waiter , he gestured , that , waiter will be attending shortly. The angel, our coveted dear waiter appeared exactly after 5 mins , & took our orders . Then my dream opportunity to clone Manish Sharma's magic arrived from no where , after Mr Angel took our order , we have to wait another significant period of time for the empty plates  to be put on our table, and then the wait was endless ; I could then suddenly discover that my chance to fulfill my musical destiny  is just a palm away , I picked up few spoons & could  play thejatarang on empty plates. I am enclosing some pic of empty cutleries , sadly none of my compatriots endorsed and like my idea of playing the instrument, so they have not taken my pic during the performance.
Finally the dishes arrived , the afghani pulaow was tasteless , mutton boti kabab pieces to be discovered under a microscope , hariyali chicken was boiled chicken in a green paste , the chicken biriyani was  ordinary to say the least , the only good part was "Mutton Chap" , it was delicious. In between the meal we have to wait and wait for even a glass of water, for a spoon , for a coke and for so many small things . The final amazement came in the form of bill , we have to pay a hefty price for an ordinary meal & service . I will still thank Arsalan Management for giving me the opportunity to achieve my dream of cloning my respected musician.

2015-06-11 13:24:45
Partha Dutt
30025204
4.0
Great Mughlai (Lucknow type) place. With great Biryani, kebabs, chnaap, korma and a lot more.

Pros
1. Great food. Especially biryani, half the population can swear by their biriyani. Its absolutely brilliant.
2. Great location, bang on Park Circus crossing.
3. Massive portions. Its feasible to feed two average persons off one serving.
4. Decent prices.

Cons.
1. Mildly difficult to get parking, although the security does help you considerably.
2. If you are planning to visit on a weekend or on a holiday, be prepared to be in a que for about 30mins. (The wait is worth the food).
3. The food may be a wee bit oily, so if you are on diet ask for a less oily portion.

Overall, a foodies paradise.

Arsalan, on hearing this name, the very first imagery that comes to your mind is Kebabs! Yes, you get Kolkata's most exotic kebabs over here only. Next comes Biryani with their celebrated Chap. You can go for either Chicken or Mutton because both are awesome! So, for the Lucknowi delicacy, Arsalan should be your next choice. Happy Dining! :)

2015-04-14 22:27:10

4.0
So, a restaurant like Arsalan doesn't really need a review. It's on Zomato's list of brilliant Kolkata biriyani and the name of Arsalan has become synonymous with Kolkata biriyani.
However, I would still write a few words about the fish biriyani which I got delivered to my place a few days back. ##

2015-04-13 11:17:19
Sabyasachi Raychaudhuri  (Foodaholix.in)
260065
4.0
Kolkata is known all over India for its version of Mughlai cuisine. The cuisine is a combination from the kitchens of  Awadh (stemming from the chefs of Nawab Wajed Ali Shah, who was detained here by the British), Muslim chefs from UP/Bihar as well as the Nawabi cuisine of Murshidabad. The restaurant which has got iconic status serving this food is Arsalan at Park Circus.

On a Sunday afternoon, there was a queue of waiting people on the footpath in front of the restaurant which is bang on the Park Circus crossing. It took around 15 minutes to be ushered upstairs to a table. The place was congested, not well lit, with a funny blue lighting.  Since we were clear about what we wanted to order, it did not take much time for the food to be served.

The Special Mutton Biryani was fragrant and mild. It is a huge departure from the spicy Hyderabadi version which I am accustomed to. The biryani had two pieces of medium sized soft and succulent mutton, one large potato and one egg. The long grained basmati rice had the flavor of ghee and kewra water, and did not leave an aftertaste of vanaspati which is the norm with many places serving Kolkata biryani.

The Mutton Chaap and Mutton Rezala were the other dishes we ordered and they did not disappoint at all. The sweet and sour curd and cashew based gravy of the rezala soaked into the soft tandoori roti was sheer heavenly, and the spicy and oily chap found its perfect foil in the roomali. At Rs 700, Arsalan provided another unforgettable experience which I will savour till I come back next

4.0
This place needs no introduction. Not just localites, people come here to have their biryani from other states too. Located in crowded park circus area this place always packed and filled with tons of hungry customers and impatient energy. The dine in facility is average and most people go for parcel facility so that they can take home and cherish their kebabs and biryaanis. The service is pretty fast considering the crowd.

Coming to their Biryaani, i am not very fond of them as i have had better and extremely yum biryaani in kashmir and Delhi. More than the biryaani i have heard people talk very highly of their quality of rice which is longer than usual basmati and that it is their speciality. Anyways but if you ask me i find the taste just normal.

Coming to their mutton chanp- now thats a show stoppper. Extremely tasty very well done and blended. I just wish they could make it boneless as the bones come on the way and you cant cherish the item to the fullest.

Their malai chicken kebab, tandoori and mutton kakori was just yum. i would say their mughlai items are really mouth watering and pocket friendly too.¬†

Good news is that they deliver in plenty of areas. I live in kasba and they agreed to deliver whenever and specifically mentioned that they have expanded their deliverable areas. However that does not mean new town or rajarhaat so those living in these areas will have to check with arsalaan.

Overall i think this place does serve quality and quantity food and they have only happy customers.

Lets say..I drooled on the Biryani and the taste dangled on my tongue pretty much enough to pull me again to Arsalan inspite of it being crowded and not in perfect ambiance!

Located in the heart of Kolkata, Arsalan redefines Biryani. Especially for those who are not from the city. The first time I tried Arsalan Biryani, I did not like it. For someone who was used to eating Thalappakatti Biryani in Chennai, it was a 180 degree U-turn. I was shocked to see a huge Aloo sitting in my biryani and staring at me. I mocked my Bengali friends - "Who puts Aloo in the Biryani??". Also, having the same without raita was another shock. After few days, I discovered its amazing taste and I have to admit that me and this Arsalan Biryani are something more than friends. Now it has become a part of my life and I travel almost 10 kms to Arsalan every week to eat here.

This place is amazing not only for the great food, but also because it captures the true charm of Kolkata. Located in the crowded Park Circus area, this place is like a shrine for Kolkata food lovers. At times I think Bengalis don't miss home food as much as they miss the Arsalan madness.¬†

My list of recommendations includes:

Mutton Rezala¬†
Mutton Kakori Kebab
Tandoori Chicken
Mutton Pasinda
Mutton Arsalan Special
Murgh Mussallam (with Kabuli Naan)
Phirni (for desserts)

My list of favorites is long and that is the only issue with this place. I have to struggle to chose which ones to order. The place is amazing because of it's excellent food and all the associated imperfections (crowded, loud and everything). If you are there in the holy month of Ramadan, make sure that you go there in the afternoon for some Halim.

Now coming to the ambience,the non-ac section is just like any roadside eatery-small and cramped, but the foos made up for it. Believe me, nothing in the world is as beautiful as four deliciously cooked chicken leg pieces in front of you. The chicken tangris were tender, juicy and was a little bit charred which actually tasted like heaven. I am surely going back soon to try the other dishes.

2015-03-22 16:34:38
Satyaki Sensarma
3213426
4.0
Arsalan is probably the first name when we talk about biriyani at Kolkata. Legendary brand name. They are consistently serving biriyani and other Mughal delicacies with a super fine quality at super reasonable price. I am a regular customer and whenever I go there I cannot resist myself from ordering a plate of mutton biriyani. Fine long grained rice, minimum amount of oil, very well cooked piece of meat, no rice grain combined together to make even a small chunk, heavenly aroma and mouth watering taste makes it one of the "don't miss" delicacies of the city. All the Mughal dishes maintain the same standard. However, got surprised to notice in the menu card that they are also offering some so called Indian Chinese dishes as well! This is something I would not appreciate. I believe, Arsalan is already so distinguished for their Mughal cuisine that they do not need any other cuisine to support the business; rather the flavours of Chinese and Mughal dishes are so conflicting that they should not be cooked and served under the same dine in roof - harmful to each other.
Dine in facility is averagely decorated. Ground floor is non ac and first floor is ac. Ground floor is always over crowded and full of noise, also too hot to enjoy the food during summer as the kitchen is just adjacent. Ac floor seems to be more peaceful.
I, last day had a long chat with the person sitting at the cash counter; not sure if he was the owner or co-owner. I wanted to get some idea of their Mutton Lucknowi biriyani. He was extremely frank and friendly to explain it in detail. I ordered it and liked it as well. It was a very pleasant experience for me.

Hearing this, almost all the others dived down in a plate of biriyani, but I for myself was never a biriyani fan. So after long pondering I went for rumali rotis and a plate of chicken reshmi butter masala. Now this is a dish I often order at various restaurants, and on that evening I was not feeling up to trying the unknown. I had reasonable ideas about how the dish might taste, and was happy with that. However, though they surely took their own sweet time to deliver the rumali rotis, as soon as I took the first bite, I was in heaven. That chicken was unlike any of the other variations I tasted, and to be honest it ruined that dish for me. After tasting their preparation, the couple times I tried to order it from any other restaurant, it seemed bland and tasteless. Besides that chicken reshmi butter masala all the items seemed to pale. I tasted some of chicken arsalan masala, which was good too, and had pineapples in the dish. As for the sweet tooths, the firni however, was a downer. It was just okay, nothing over the top, and seemed almost not worth the 40 bucks. However I'm sure I'm going to be back for the chicken. Pocket pinch was very light, 1100 for six. All in all, a worthy experience.

##

2015-02-25 19:15:44
Anindita Ghosh
1025083
4.5
Arsalan defines Kolkata style Biryani. It's like "kolkata te biryani bhalo kothaye?" and 90% of bongs would take the name of Arsalan in one shot. 
Birthdays, parties, anniversaries or any other kind of treats are incomplete without the scrumptious, oily, tasty and fragrant Biryani of Arsalan.
According to my knowledge, during famine in Bengal people started cooking potatoes with rice so that it could fill their stomach, helping them to struggle their hunger for a longer period of time. That tradition is still being followed by adding potatoes in kolkata style biryanis. The person who came up with this idea was a genius! I dont know how they manage to incorporate that amazing taste in the aloo (potato) of their biryani. The meat pieces are equally good in size and well cooked. The rice used is of good quality and the taste is one of a kind. 
The chicken chaap and mutton chaap are pretty good and both are too oily but all tasty things are not healthy.
However, I don't like their cheese kebabs. I love cheese, be it any kind but these kebabs are so heavily loaded with cheese that after sometime of eating these, it becomes very difficult to gulp'em down (kind of uneasy feeling inside the stomach).

I love the firnis they serve!

In all, Biryani is what has made Arsalan famous and be it anyday from Monday to Sunday this place remains jam packed. 

Totally Recommended. 
Happy eating! :D

##

2015-02-02 03:13:22
Sumitavo Paul
183369
4.5
I started visiting Arsalan from 2002 - the year when it was opened. Walking distance from my college, Arsalan in 2002 used to serve the cheapest food in Park Street-Park Circus area. But the days of 30/- Biryani and 20/- Chicken Dopiyaza are gone now. Arsalan is now the most coveted Mughlaai restaurant in Kolkata with branches all over the city. The busiest of them all is the main one at Park Circus 7-point crossing - the lower level with no a/c is my favourite as I used to enjoy the oily and spicy foods with my friends fighting over dishes.

The best of the menu card is obviously the mutton biryani - the spicy rice, tender big chunk of muttona and the big potato - all blend together very well. Among the mutton dishes - Kassa, Qorma, Mutton masala, dahi mutton, pasinda, mutton kali mirch (a spicy version), mutton do piyaza, mutton rogan josh all are very good, but my favourite is the mutton champ - less bone than most of the kolkata restaurants. The mutton champ with the tawa hot roomali roti is a delicacy.

Chicken chaap, kashmiri, qorma, lahori murg, chicken boneless masala, tikka/reshmi/tandoori butter masala all are very good.

The items from tandoor are also very good - chicken boti, chicken tikka, mutton boti, mutton bara, fish tandoori all are mouth watering.

I have tried lachha paratha, butter naan, kabuli naan, keema naan, roomali roti - which are very good and goes well with the kebabs/gravy items.

One word of caution - like all mughlaai joints, all gravy items are extremely oily and spicy. So check your health graph before digging into them.

Also if you like to get a sophisticated and better presentation and better ambience, go for the outlet below the AJC Bose flyover or the one at Park Street area.

Lastly - this is hugely recommended to all my friends.

Go for it and enjoy the food !

Went to Arsalan for dinner after having starters at Woldork, so were almost full. But the smell of authentic biriyani made us hungry as soon as we entered the place. After the heavy dinner came the desserts time. And when at Arsalan you need to have their firni and gajar ka halwa. Firni cool as ever with that perfect taste and hot gajar ka halwa with loads of ghee to compliment it. 
Had a good time at the place. Dont even remember how many times have i visited the place but surely gonna visit it a hundreds of time more before cholesterol kills me.

We (there were four of us) reached Arsalan at around 8:00pm on Christmas night after a long long walk from Park Street. There was a queue in front of the restaurant. We were customer number 62 in the queue.

I am a comfort loving person and always tend to avoid crowd and hustle and bustle. That‚Äôs the reason I normally tend to avoid going out during Durga Puja and all such occasions when there is a possibility of getting pushed around.

Arsalan queue moved in front of the restaurant like a 1000 foot snake which moved slowly but systematically. I have to give credit to Arsalan management for managing the festive crowd and they ensured the entire affair was systematically done. After standing in the queue for about 45 minutes, we were able to get our desired table at the AC restaurant on the first floor. For people yet to pay a visit to Arsalan, you have two sitting options ‚Äì Ground floor (non-AC) and first floor(with AC).

We took the seat and immediately placed the following order. We were all immensely hungry after the marathon walk.

Mutton Biriyani Special(2 pieces) ‚Äì Rs. 225.00/-Chicken Biriyani ‚Äì Rs. 150/-Mutton Rogan Josh(3 Pieces) ‚Äì Rs. 195/-Chicken Reshmi Butter Masala(6 pieces) ‚Äì Rs 200/-Chicken Bharta (shredded) ‚Äì Rs. 120/-

It was a short wait and then it was served. It was just pure heaven in a plate. The taste of all the items was excellent and biriyani was just out of this world. I have had multiple arguments with my friends that Arsalan Biriyani was best in the city. It was a great dinner.

2014-11-28 20:03:18
Saswati Banerjee
1308434
4.0
There are restaurants that serve authentic and delectable food, and then there are restaurants that simply carry forward a legacy, they are legendary. Since the day I stepped into Kolkata and mentioned Biryani in a discussion, I remember being asked, irrespective by whom or where, have you eaten at Arsalan? Today I‚Äôm glad that I did. 

Located at Park Circus, Arsenal requires no introduction whatsoever. As soon as you enter, you‚Äôre welcomed by the mouthwatering whiff of kebabs and rich Biryanis being grilled and cooked in bulk. There is a non AC seating arrangement downstairs and an air conditioned restaurant upstairs, hence enabling you to choose according to your comfort. The place is crowded all the time and if you‚Äôre looking out for a place to sit, a lill sacrifice and compromise on time is inevitable. The restaurant interiors are decent, nothing eye striking but not bad either. There‚Äôs always a hustle bustle kind of atmosphere, with people working and screaming out orders at jet speed. 

The food. Arsalan is known to serve unsurpassed Biryanis in town. How could I differ on that? It indeed serves ones of the finest Biryanis, long grains of rice; it‚Äôs not too dry nor is it loaded with excess oil or dalda . It‚Äôs just level perfectness. The quantity of rice served is ample and it goes without mentioning that their Biryanis are simply delicious, spot on. Probably due to excess hunger we ordered once each of Chicken, Mutton and Egg Biryani, and once again each of them was scrumptious. In their gravy items I loved the Murgh Makhani- a rich red gravy lip smacking chicken preparation with a dollop of cream on the top, which will compliment your bread and rice perfectly. Their kebabs are undoubtedly delicious with that splendid smoky flavor. Their service is amazingly quick, there is hardly any delay. Prices are affordable, maybe a tad more than other Biryani houses, yet totally worth it.

Like any other attraction in town, Arsalan probably is a must visit if you ever come to Kolkata. It celebrates food, rich and royal North Indian and Mughlai Cuisine. It‚Äôs one experience every foodie must have. Guess food itself, speaks so much better than words ;) Kudos!

decent service this time, we had some bitter experiences before. Once they

asked for more tip when one of our friends was not courteous enough to offer
him a proper tip. But these hiccups are worth the amazing and authentic Mughlai
food they offer and they won't deter us from visiting Arsalan again.

2014-11-08 21:43:55
Ritinkar Dasbhaumik
10366431
1.0
I'm not really sure why this restaurant is rated a 4.2. 
I tend to judge such restaurants in Calcutta on the basis of two dishes, the biryani and the chaap.
The biryani first: The rice is light, not very flavourful. Not great, but not terrible either. Things start to fall apart as I turn to the chicken; the meat is stale with clear dark marks of discolouration. Not very appetising. The mutton biryani is better. Stick to it.
So far, I'd give it a 2.0 or a 2.5. Why the 1.0?
The chaap. 
Arsalan's chaap is by some margin, the worst among the big 'Mughlai' restaurants in Calcutta. The staleness issue persists, but what does it for me is the unusual sourness that one gets with the very first bite. It's not a slight tanginess, but very in your face like someone had doused the pan in a lot of vinegar. Not just does this  block out every spice in the dish, but it is incredibly nauseating. 
Now, a lot of people love this restaurant, and I hear the kebabs are good. Perhaps this is true, but I wouldn't go back for them. Not if the biryani and chaap are anything to go by. 
If you're in the Park Circus area and you must have biryani and chaap, go to Zeeshan or Shiraz. Give this place a miss.
If you must dine at Arsalan, stick to mutton.

I would recommend this place highly, specially for those who are new to Calcutta and would want to get a feel of the legendary 'Calcutta Style Biryani'.

food: food is superb fotlr the price you pay for. specially the biriyani and the kebabs. as of me, this is the best biriyani house in kolkata. smooth long rice, well cooked tender mutton and the oh-so-great aroma! its mouth watrering! same goea for kebabs and tandoor dishes like tikka, reschmi, hariyali kebab and chiken tandoori. however for side dishes like chaanp or bharta there is definitely room for improvement. 

ambience and service: if you would rather ear average food in a greatly decorated place arsalan is not for you. there is noise, service is, too, not up to the mark. personally i dont care if the food served is good enough.

price: price is obviously the biggest advantage for arsalan. food of this quality at this price is unbelivable.

so this is one of the best place to have biryani or kebabs( or both as is the case for me often)! a must visit for all food lovers.

Arguably considered my many, as Kolkata's "best biriyani" restaurant, Arsalan has certainly made a name for themselves over the past few years.. The biriyani indeed tastes great, and would not go into the details of it.. However, the Mutton Lucknow Biriyani, be guarded, is extremely spicy, and tastes a lot different from the average biriyanis we have in Kolkata.. As for the biriyani again, one thing I would like to point out is the excessive amount of oil they use in their signature dish.. It's really disappointing, and hope they would look into that..
The best dish of their restaurant, their Malai Kebab, their special Chicken Kebab, is just heavenly.. Wrapped in cheese, it would melt away in your mouth and you would still yearn for more even after three helpings.. Undoubtedly the best kebab I have had in Kolkata..

2014-09-17 13:24:47
Manish Menghani
177222
4.0
Whenever you get a chance to visit Kolkata, this is the place to be! If you like Non-vegetarian food - Arsalan has been one of the most consistent restaurants in the city.¬† I visited the restaurant during lunch on a Friday noon - it was jam-packed - there were about 18 people waiting to be seated and it took me around 45 minutes to just manage a table for two!¬† 

We managed to get¬† a seat but that is not all - I didn't quit like the idea and spacing of the interiors of the restaurant - tables are too close-by! The ambiance of the restaurant is decent if you sit downstairs, with those yellow lights but if you manage a table upstairs, you'll be welcomed with the kinetic blue lights allover, it is dark!

I began with the finest starter that is - Chicken Arsalan, essentially it is Chicken marinated in mild spices and wrapped with melted Cheese. Tasted amazingly balanced with the Jeera Raita they serve. The latter is something you'll probably find nowhere except at Arsalan's - must try!

For mains, I ordered for the very popular Chicken Biryani, made Kolkata style and I felt it was perfectly cooked, with minimal spices and the taste being absolutely balanced. Generally, Biryanis are spicy and not many of us can handle the spice, sometimes but this one here is a toned-down version of the Chicken Biryani served in Hyderabad or Lucknow!

Whenever I am in Kolkata, I will definitely visit the place again. Such joy!

Service: 3.5/5
Food: 4.2/5
Ambiance: 3/5
Value for Money: 3.5/5

Situated in close proximity to the Seven-Point Crossing of Park Circus, this food joint could never be of any inconvenience to any Biryani lover/connoisseur. The ground floor has no AC, but the First floor is totally air-conditioned. Quite noted for its authentic Biryani in Calcutta, the other dishes in this food joint are worth trying out. Notable among them are all the chicken and mutton kababs, the rotis and the nuns. Home Delivery is also available with this outlet.
¬†It opened around late 2002, but still today, they have maintained their authenticity and the quality of their dishes. Use of ersatz colors in biryanis here to make profit from the customers is out of practice since its inception.¬†The texture of the biryanis is entirely different from the ones one would find elsewhere. The kababs, seasoned with lime, gets enriched in taste.¬†
The staffs are well-behaved and amiable; they carry about their person a certain code of dignity. The prices are reasonable and one would never feel a pinch in their pockets. Overall, with a very high-spirited ambiance and jovial nature of the staffs, this place is definitely a one to drop in and to savour the finest items available here.

##

2014-07-04 16:52:01
Rishav Dey
193398
3.5
Arsalan, without a shadow of doubt is good. But in my humble opinion it is over rated. It is good but not excellent. Their biryanis are good. The mutton special biryani and the mutton Lucknowi biryani are their best in my opinion. The chicken ones are not bad. But at some point of time they used 'less-oil' as their U.S.P. Now I doubt if they can lay claim to that. Not only are the biryanis oily, after gulping down one mouthful of biryani the top of the mouth remains coated with oil. It probably is not the best quality oil either. But this is probably expected of a place like Arsalan. The biryani is good but in my opinion not Kolkata's best. 
The kebabs are good as well.Some of my personal favourites are the chicken tikka, tengdi, garlic, kakori and the mutton boti, barra, and kakori. The best of the lot are definitely the Arsalan kebabs with cheese atop the kebabs. They just add a  different flavour to the kebabs.
The chicken kadai and the lahori chicken are really good. Both are extremely rich and spicy. The rezala is amazing. It tastes rather well and is yet quite light. The mutton rezala si good as well but they hardly ever serve good pieces. The kebabs in butter masala are good but nothing special. The mutton dahi and the mutton stew are two of my favourties in Arsalan. But the mutton rogan josh stands out. It somehow reminds me of the rogan josh which used to served in the railway canteens and Rajdhani trains quite some time back.
The lachha paratha and tandoori roti are not advised if you are taking away food otherwise go ahead and help yourself. The butter naan and the romali roti remain soft even after they get cold. And make sure you don't miss their phirni. Although the prices have increased manifolds in recent times but one can't really blame them, the value for money remains high.
