2014-07-02 02:51:05
Sunny Ali
1594046
4.5
I have had the pleasure of tasting Mughlai Cuisines across many Restaurants in Kolkata, but, to me, if I had to chose one Restaurant that stands out with its Lip-smacking Delicacies, then it has to be Arsalan (Park Circus, Kolkata).
Conveniently located in 'the Heart of the City', the Restaurant is approachable from any corner of the City. Although, it has opened up many Branches, it is the Park Circus venue that dishes out the Best Biriyanis in Kolkata.
The Restaurant is divided into 2 sections: Non-AC (Ground Floor) and AC (First Floor) seating. One will find it difficult to find a seat during Rush Hours (Read: From Noon to Night) and especially on Festive occasions. However, when one does find a seat, its an Experience worth Waiting for!
To me, the Best Dish on the Menu and my most Frequent order, is the Arsalan Mutton Special Biriyani. With succulent pieces of Mutton and oodles of Taste, it will take you to a different world of Culinary Pleasure! Although all the Kebabs are good, but one should definitely try the 'Arsalan Special Kebab'! But Beware, its not for the Calorie Conscious foodies!
The Service is prompt and is taken care by Seasoned Hands, who are willing to change the mutton / chicken piece in your Biriyani, if you are not happy with it!!!!
The only drawback I can think of is maybe the Cleanliness. With hundreds of Visitors each day, hygiene, at times, takes a hit, with not so clean tables and glasses, which again can be cleaned and changed on request.
To sum it up, it is 'the Place' to go, if you want a feel of Authentic Mughlai Food!

2014-06-20 00:33:49
Sreeparna Dutta
1637264
5.0
Arsalan serves the best Biriyani in Kolkata and I have been here for about nth times on the pretext of any small occasion just to taste its Biriyani. Here goes my review ( Park Circus branch):
 
Ambiance= Pathetic. (Rating: 1/5)
I saw people eating Biriyani here, as if they did not eat food for the past 7 days! 365 days in a year there will be mad rush of customers. By looking at the 'serpentine' queue outside (for Take away) it seems that people are queuing up to enter into a puja pandal!  Inside, there is too much noise and chaos - too much congested and less space. 

Service= Mediocre. (Rating: 2/5)
Waiters are running here and there, look puzzled and loosing track of the orders placed. Always in a hurry and sweating badly (even in AC). They will come many times to check whether you are done or not (since there is always a huge queue) and will indirectly tell you to leave by handing over the bill much before you finished the food.

Food= Scrumptious. (Rating: 5/5)
Food is the only reason why Arsalan is so famous. It serves the best Biriyani in Kolkata. Don't have much idea about the other items because 99% people come here to have its Biriyani for which it is so famous for. Arsalan ka Biriyani is the best Biriyani that I have ever tasted in my whole life. I don't need anything else if I have Arsalan's Biriyani with Chicken Chap and Firni. It's simply finger-licking good.

Value for money= Reasonable (4/5)
The price is a bit on the higher side but still I will consider it as reasonable only because of the quality of the Biriyani and food that they serve.

Overall I rated it 5 and this is only for the 'Arsalan ka Biriyani'

2014-06-15 20:12:28

4.5
Being a great biriyani lover,  i dont remember how many times i have visited Arsalan ..... infact i have lost the count long ago after 10 ...... :)
To me , they are the best biriyani makers in kolkata as of now ....... i have tasted dada-boudi biriyani, aminia, shiraz , lazeez, hanglatherium, and almost all other strong competitors  in kolkata multiple times ..... but arsalan stands out from the rest ...... i am never bored of eating biriyani here ........ they do strong justice to their brand name .......
Other than  biriyani, the next point that deserves mention here is their kebabs section specially tandoori chicken ...... often in most places u would find the tandoori pieces not being uniformly roasted ...some parts are overcooked and some are raw in a single piece of tandoori chicken ..... but here in Arsalan whenever i have ordered tandoori, i found the whole tandoori being uniformly cooked/roasted ,and never otherwise ........
The PRICE is standard i should say ...... a normal mutton biriyani would cost u approx 150-160rs ..... special biriyani around 240rs .....which is value for money compared to so many costly restuarants in the city ....... 
Other than the above mentioned points, everything else is ordinary ....... i.e the side dishes are average ....not bad not exceptional .... infact most of them very oily ..... u can see literally oil floating in the dish alongside thick gravy ........ the staff behaviour is not that good ...... place is very congested inside ...in both the AC and the nonAC sections ....... ambience is though slightly better in AC section .......

But still , its just becoz of their biriyani, i like to visit it over and over again ......

2014-05-26 23:36:49
Saket Sharma
325323
4.5
There are some places in India where anybody from anywhere would come and will fall in love with the culture, people and food. Food is one of the reason I would visit calcutta anyday and the kohinoor of this city comes as Arsalan. Even being veggie, I can't complain about anything here.

Its not a 5 star hotel or anything like that, a basic restaurant which knows the need of common people. You visit such place and just become a fan. I heard about Arsalan in my last trip, but didn't get chance that time and i.e. forced my group to visit this time.

So we 4 people reached there in evening time and place is overcrowded and I got to know its the everyday story, we somehow managed to find a place for 4 after a wait of 5-10 mins, ambiance not great, this one has basic sitting on ground floor and AC one on first floor, having high humid weather outside we opted for AC one. I don't know whether rates changes or not due to that. 

Ok too much info about hotel, skipping all details :), coming to food, we ordered 2 mutton and 1 egg biryani for my non-veggie frns and 1 veg biryani for me.  As i am used to south indian biryani i thought curd is a thing which always accompany briyani, but in calcutta that is not the case.

I ordered one paneer gravy and then started our dinner and let me tell you from the first bite itself, it was something else for all of us, specially non-veggies they were just licking their fingers, they serve potatos with rice and everybody liked that combination. Quantity for one person is definitely what you can eat so no complaint there as well.

Service sometimes is bit sloppy but all sins are forgettable when you get such heavenly taste.  I don't think people order anything other than biryani here as I saw biryani on all tables, thus will say a MUST try.

When it came to bill, it was just 150RS for a biryani on avg and its completely VFM for the taste and quantity they have.

Ratings:

Ambiance : 2.5
Service: 3
Taste: 5
VFM: 4.5
Overall : 4.5 (No avg here as taste compensate for everything)

The ambience not so special (sat in the AC dining hall) and decently lighted. Over to the much hyped biryani and I asked the waiter to serve the best (arsalan special) and was suprised we had to order raitha separately since in bangalore & hyderabad they serve it for free.

The biryani had a huge piece of potato and a boiled along which even though I was aware but never liked a potato in biryani. My taste buds got the first taste of sweetness only all throughout I ate the biryani and couldn't finish the entire plate.

Only advice to people used to hyderabadi style is be prepared for a sweet biryani and lack of garam masala in the biryani and no baigan gravy you get in south india. 

Overall not a bad place for biryani but my search continues for the spicy hyderabadi biryani in the city of joy.

##

2014-04-24 05:50:26
Suman Biswas
498443
4.5
====MOST DETAILED REVIEWS====================================
Personally I visit this place more often than any other restaurant ; probably because my college is in the intimate vicinity and obviously because I am a hardcore biriyani lover. Okay its situated in the Park Circus 7 Point Crossing and most of us know that this is Sourav Ganguly's Fav Biriyani House. 

FOODS:
Only Mughlai & North Indian.
PRO- 1) The best biriyani in Kolkata. It doesn't need anyone's approval. Quantity is sufficient. Side dishes are appreciable. But all of them are quite rich and buttery. 
2) Kebabs are yummy, quite soft. And other side dishes are killer too. Ch. Reshmi Butter Masala and Ch. Tikka Butter Masala are highly recommended. 
3) Firni Is killer one here.
4) Though Zomato is writing that they sell Chinese Dishes. but I never saw any of them in Park Circus Arsalan. Even if it is available -it will not be that good, I guess.
5) Huge variations of choices in menu is available.
5) In the Take Away portion it sells Roll. Chicken Rolls are just Mind blowing. Soft and juicy. Oh yeah!! 

CON- This Restro remains busy all the time so sometimes it may take a lil longer time in case you are in the take away portion.
{rating: 5/5}

SERVICE:
PRO: All the stuffs are okay. Food is served at an affordable time gap in most of the cases.

CON: They don't have Car (4 wheeler parking area) or a waiting lounge. You have to wait outside. In the time of occasion (ex. Durga Puja, Christmas) they seem to hire inexperienced stuffs who really can irritate you at times. And in these days getting a seat can be a real pain in the rear end. 
. {rating: 3/5}

AMBIANCE:
PRO: Well, ambiance, illumination and the decoration are not up to mark. Its good for hardcore mughlai (Say Biriyani) lovers. It has a Non AC ground floor (Cheaper in terms of price.) And a AC upper floor (Costlier, Obviously). It has also a Take Away Portion in front. 

CON: All the tables have lesser gaps. Your private discussion, if any has to be done will be hampered for sure. Every time it remains congested. For family outing, Dating or romanticism-mongers- this place is not good at all. They should go to the Park Street (Beside AJC bose Flyover) Arsalan. . 
{rating: 2/5}

PRICE: Price is good. Pricing seems nice to me; if it strikes u- its because you are in Central Kolkata, it has to be this much pricey. CLUB SOLITAIRE CARD ACCEPTED with 15% rebate, only in this outlet.
{Rating: 4.0/5}

Nearby Alternative:
Arsalan Park Street (Best For Party Banquet, Family Gatherings, Date, outings etc ) in this range of price and area. 
Shiraz Park Street

ENJOY.
Happy Bengali New Year.

2014-04-22 15:01:09
Amlan Majumder
802659
4.0
This is perhaps the best outlet of Arsalan in the city. The mughlai cuisine served here is totally out of the world experience and hence is the demand of its cooked dishes which is evident by the large crowd waiting in queues for their turn for take aways and dining in. True value for money cuz the dishes served here have a sizeable portion in each serving which can serve more tham one person. Whenever I am at this restaurant (mostly during lunch hours) I always order a special mutton Biryani (contains extra rice and meat) and a mutton chaap, afyer eati g such a gigantic and heavy meal, i never feel hungry till the next 12 hours!!! Not to mention the taste, after having it, you dont feel like tasting anything else. The after taste lasts for nearly 3 hours atleast. If one tries the cuisine here, one can never feel disappointed with the food. The only downside of this restaurant is its ambience. Tables are kept very near to each other due to huge space crunch. Hence during peak hours of the day, one may not expect a comfortable sitting arrangement in its lounge for dining in. But that is supplemented by the hospitality of the waiters, thorough gentleman attitude in each of them. Only the crowded space and stuffiness in the air at its restaurant lounge is the negative point of this outlet, otherwise a great place to eat!!!
.
Edit date 1st dec 2017:
The restaurant have become very very pricey. A portion of special biryani now costs over 300 and a portion of side dish costs 200. Add taxes to it and you will be shelling over 520 per head. Aroma of the food isnt as strong as it used to be and each portion of the dishes have shrunk. Though it continues to be the best biryani outlet, its decline in quality have taken me aback.

2014-04-12 08:12:21
Udayan Das
185660
4.5
Location : At Park Circus itself

Ambiance : Above average decor. Nothing exceptional. Service average.

Food : First of all ordered the chicken Biriyani to extinguish the hunger then the Hariyali Butter Masala followed suit along with Naan and Chicken Reshmi Butter Masala. It's amazing to see how they are so dedicated to the quality of food being served. Each of the Outlets has this one thing in common : Consistency. The chicken dishes were moist and tender. Just falls apart in your mouth every time. Even the naan  was praiseworthy. Soft and aromatic to be precise. After all this carnage, the apple of my eye arrived : " Chicken Arsalan Kebab". This is a dish that I never fail to order irrespective of everything. We took it apart slowly and relished the cheesy , heavenly concoction. We were so immersed that forgot to click it's pic :P ! After all this was stuffed enough to order some Thumbs up !! All in all a great day as always. 

TIP : Be there by 11 AM or after 3 PM ! Otherwise prepare to stand in a queue in this blistering heat ! This is no doubt the most in demand outlet of Arsalan there is ! Although Arsalan devotees know this but still if you're looking to order the "Chicken Arsalan Kebab" do so while consuming your first dish because it takes half an hour to prepare and gets to you piping hot !!

Final conclusion : Not as fancy as their Park street outlet but more importantly the food is bang on here as well. At a cost for 2 of about 800/- plus it may not be the cheapest but sure is worth every last rupee . Satisfaction guranteed.

##

2014-02-12 13:05:08
Bhaswati Chakrabarti
892471
4.0
The origin of the Mughlai cuisine can be traced back to the times of the Mughal Empire. The Mughals, who invaded India in the 16th century, brought with them a treasure trove of aromatic and exotic spices, herbs and nuts that were used to prepare mouth watering dishes. The natives were predominately influenced by the Mughlai cooking and got to learn new techniques of cooking. The spices and nuts used in the preparation of Mughlai dishes made food lip smacking and enticing. It was long time back. But Mughlai cuisine is still our favourite. How often my heart craves for a plateful of biryani, chicken tandoori or succulent kebabs! And whenever I crave for the flavour of exotic spices, I head straight to Arsalan.

Arsalan is known for its style and splendour in cooking. The appropriate use of aromatic spices makes food truly delectable.  Chicken biryani, mutton kasha, mutton rogan josh, chicken rezala, chicken korma, chicken hariyali, chicken boti kebab, chicken tangri kebab and chicken malai kebab are some of the exotic dishes served at Arsalan.  The soft and succulent meat pieces and the biryani, prepared from long-grained rice are so delicious! The best part is food is neither rich, nor oily so you can enjoy your fill anytime. 

Seating can be a big problem at Arsalan, especially if you are visiting the Park Circus outlet. The place is too crammed up. But you can always carry your food home.  All Arsalan outlets are over crowded during the festive season with foodies craving for more and more exotic cuisine. However, you can drop in anytime to enjoy some lip smacking food.

##

2014-02-12 09:25:19
Suman Mandal
369651
2.5
Last night I visited this place and it was a complete letdown.

We went there after a long day. Having been eating nothing but Biriyani and Kebabs here previously, we thought to try some other dishes. But it seemed that the staff was not even interested in taking our order so much so that we had to call someone just to get the menu. Then when we asked the waiter for some suggestion about what we should try he simply said one or two names reluctantly and went on his way.

At last we decided to go for 2 Tandoori Rotis, 1 Chicken Boneless Masala and 1 Mutton Biriyani. Surprisingly, the order came through as 2 Tandoori Rotis and 1 Butter Nan accompanied by the Boneless Chicken Masala- 1 Nan too many. We told them that we didn't order the Nan and then only they took it back.

After finishing the Tandoori Rotis we were waiting for the Biriyani. And again another surprise- Our order for Mutton Biriyani simply didn't reach the kitchen. The waiter just ignored it somehow. They took our order separately for the Biriyani and served it.

One notable thing is that when they understood that our order was not conveyed to the kitchen correctly the waiter did get a bit of criticism, if not scolding, from the other staffs (We were not able to make out what exactly were spoken). But I really doubt if that's gonna have a long-term effect.

When it comes to the quality of the food, it was great. I haven't got such nice Tandoori Rotis in Kolkata for quite some time now. They were fresh out of the oven as opposed to the "Cooked-long-ago-and-heated-on-oven-before-serving" type we generally encounter in the city. The Boneless Chicken was also awesome. Spicy Boneless Chicken pieces surrounded by a thick gravy and topped off by Fresh Cream- only a handful of restaurants can compete against this superb delicacy.

And the Mutton Biriyani was also another great produce of Arsalan Kitchen. The texture, the flavor- nothing to complain.

Then came the bill and yet another surprise. They have charged us for even the Butter Nan we didn't order and later returned. Again we informed them of it and they promptly struck off the item from the bill. We paid and came back.

At the end, I reckon it was a good decision for us to try dishes other than Biriyanis and Kebabs here. The Tandoori Roti and Boneless Chicken Masala filled up my mind as much as my stomach. Their Biriyani was, is and hopefully remain as Kolkata's one of the best, if not THE Best. I thought of upgrading them due to their expertise in dishes other than their traditional strong points.

But unfortunately, the service actually compelled me to downgrade them a bit. A restaurant of such promises that Arsalan holds can not excel much with this kind of service. Yesterday they were severely understaffed which is becoming a common trade here day by day. Separate people to take the order and serving the food can easily create misunderstandings like what happened with us. The waiters also need to be warm. Customers do not mind to repeat their orders and but they become a lot disapproving toward the restaurant to receive the wrong food. Now that their food is really gaining attention from a lot of people, Arsalan management need to focus on the service sector more. It's for them to decide if they want to be in the long run or fall from grace rather quickly and become merely another milestone in the history of Kolkata Eateries.



----- 21 Jan, 2014 -----

Third time here and I understood the secret of being here and get amazed- I am not going to  try their Mutton dishes again, ever.

My friends ordered a Mutton Biriyani and I decided to taste their Mutton Tikka Kebab. As usual, the biriyani was great, nothing to say in that sector. Service was good and the ambiance was also great this time.

However, the mutton pieces were hard. Even cutting them with teeth required a great deal of effort. The Kebabs had the right spices in the right amount but it was all in vain since the mutton pieces were not even nearly chew-able.

On the other hand, the Firni was great, I must admit.

Basically, except for the mutton pieces, it was a great experience. But the Mutton made it a complete disaster.



----- 14 Jan, 2014 -----

So, I visited this place once again but this time I am somewhat disappointed.

As soon as we got there, we noticed a number of people waiting outside. Fortunately, a two-seated table emptied quickly and we were led to the Air Conditioned 1st floor. The lighting, decoration and the furnishing was nice and soothing but it was a bit crowded. Felt like they put a table wherever they could. Customers as well as the Waiters faced problem moving around. But once one settles down, it was all good.

When we ordered Lucknow Biriyani, the waiter, for some unknown reasons, tried to discourage us by telling it was oily, spicy etc. At last we ordered a Special Mutton Biriyani and one plate of Kakori Kebabs.

The Biriyani came fast enough but somehow they did not even think about serving it on our plates. We had to take it up by spoon from the center plate.

But it is Arsalan and there is no need to tell how it was. Arsalan never felt to mesmerize with their Biriyanis. Be it the spices, the cooking or the oiliness, Arsalan produces one of Kolkata's best Biriyanis, time and again. On the other hand, the mutton pieces were a bit disappoint today. They were tender to chew, of course, but hard to cut down to small pieces before eating. Beyond that, it was all nice and great. The quantity and quality of the Biriyani easily made us forgive the little shortcoming of the mutton.

The Kebabs were a whole different story. I have heard great things about Arsalan's Kakori Kebabs so I thought to give it a try today. They took a long time to serve this dish (it arrived even long after we finished our biriyani) and it tasted like nothing that can be expected from Arsalan. In simple language, I did not like it. It tasted like cardamon in each bite. There was no tingling effect that is expected in Kebabs. It was a total disaster.

However, at the end, there is only one thing to say. Whatever shortcomings Arsalan may have, their Biriyani is reason enough to take me back there anytime.



----- 09 Mar, 2013 -----

Today i went to this place with my girlfriend and it was again proved that Arsalan IS Kolkata's best biriyani joint.

It's a little place but nice and cozy. I heard that the waiters are a bit rude but my experience was entirely different. We ordered one plate each of Lucknowi Biriyani and Reshmi Kabab. The service was pretty quick and they divided it equally and served to both of us even before asking them to do so.

At first I thought the price was a bit over rated, but had to change my opinion as soon as I saw the quantity. I mean, for two persons, it's cheaper than most local restaurants in Kolkata and suburbs.

And as for the quaIity, all I can say is that I have had the oportunity to taste real Lucknowi Biriyani at Lucknow itself and this was the first time I got that authentic taste in Kolkata.

The kabab was better than most of Kolkata restaurants but still it was not as good as the Biriyani. In my opinion, they should give a bit more attention to that section. Of course, it was unfortunate for me that the Kakori kababs were not available at that time.

All in all, a pretty good experience for the both of us. THUMBS UP.

2014-01-01 13:20:31
Rimjhim
1545794
5.0
Arsalan is a place where I think experiments get conducted regularly about how to make Biryani all the more better than the previous version  and transform it to another level of being a god of non-veg food. Arsalan, specially the Park Circus branch is a competition to itself only-nobody even dares to go near the legendary mark-line drawn by it in the history of making the best Biryani.

The ethereal smell will make anyone crazy at a very basic salivary level of appetite. Each and every spice(ghee-fried-onion, garam-masala etc.) can be recognized inside the mouth. And the flavor is just a dynamite of delight exploding on the taste buds. The meat is of a good texture and is well-cooked. And the rice is excuisite, none of them are broken or over bolied. Arsalan makes it sure that each time you are served with a masterpiece of its own out-of-the-world level.

For the side dishes, special mention should be made for rezala. The warm hint of pepper and the light gravy is perfect in a cold wintry evening.

Special mention for tiny bites are each and every roll of this place. You can pick any roll and munch it inside within no time in a busy schedule. No exaggeration of sauces but a good filling and well-made paratha-cover is a mouth watering delight for the fast-goers.

People visiting Kolkata 'have to' check this place out apart from Victoria Memorial or Birla Planetarium. It is as much important as the other worth-visiting kolkata spots are.

For old timers like me, Arsalan is the new kid on the block. I first went to the Park Circus joint about 6/7 years back and was introduced by a friend. Since then, it has been a regular place for me and all my guests who come to Kolkata. In fact, I suspect that several of my friends come to Kolkata more for the meal at Arsalan than for some real business with me!! Arsalan has a nice cozy restaurant and dining area which is a ctually the ground floor of a old residential house and one can make out the layout from the walls and their angles. However, I feel this adds to the ambience and feel of the place and adds to the magnificent stuff they serve. The Mutton Biriyani is the best in town.... period. But, I would rush to add here that there are several other dishes which I feel are either best or near about best in town. Try the Mutton Stew- it is a thick gravy with succulent pieces of mutton superbly diced and cooked to perfection. The Tandoori Roti is a very good too. The Chicken Biriyani has a very calm and comfortable feel about it and the Mutton Biriyani is just smooth as silk, the meat is cooked to perfection and the rice simply blends with the meat and potato. The Mutton Chaanp is also not to be missed. I always have a Menu tucked in my car or at home and they have very efficient parcel service.

Recent review 2nd Feb : thoroughly disappointed. The mutton bhoona was re heated and hard, the biriyani soggy..... EXTREMELY POOR service..... Perhaps will not come back....

4.5
Arsalan is the newest biriyani maker of the city. But has made such an impact that has put the others virtually out of business!

This place is never empty and you find at least 10-15 people buzzing and waiting, and i'm talking about deliveries. 
It has a non ac sitting arrangement downstairs, that you might squeez in to, but the ac area upstairs is never empty!
We ordered Mutton Biriyani and Chicken Butter Masala.

Anyway, coming to the food. Biriyani, is their USP. It is top notch, rich and the basmati is long and filled with flavour. The rich herb spices in the biriyani make for an everlasting footprint in your tongue that stays with you forever. The portion of mutton was big, soft and riddled with spices. The mutton was so soft that you don't even have to chew it properly! 
The Chciocken butter masala, was rich again. Bubbling flavours, the aroma...the blend of rich spices with a gravy made of onion is perfect to compliment an equally good biriyani.

I don't generally say this, but Arsalan is Horribly good. So good, that you would not settle for biriyani from any other place than this. So come here at your own risk, a risk..i feel isn't that risky to take.

##

2013-10-20 11:58:13
Ankur Banik
737186
5.0
Located unmistakably at the park circus seven point,this is for me the best outlet of Arsalan.The long queue of people waiting to get a seat at all most all times of the day is testimony to the quality and popularity of the place.

This outlet has a non ac section in the ground floor and an ac section upstairs.The non ac section in the ground floor is very hot and is too uncomfortable to try.Also here you will probably have to share your table with others.Upstairs is more like a restaurant with ac and separate tables.But thats about it.There is nothing much to write about ambience n decor.The tables are very close to each other and it is always crowded and noisy.

There is nothing to say that has probably not been said yet about the food at Arsalan.For quite a lot of people Arsalan serves the best biryani in town.I do share this opinion too.The biryani is very tasty.The pieces of chicken or mutton are also generally nice.The Hyderabadi and the Lucknow biryanis are also very good and tasty and authentic.Some people find the biryani here too oily.I do not disagree completely but I for one do not mind.The Chicken chap,mutton chap and the tandoori chicken gravy here are also excellent and must try.And who can forget the chicken arsalan kabab.Its the tastiest and best kabab I have ever had,anywhere.The wonderfully prepared chicken kabab wrapped in cheese is a treat to the taste buds.The kekuri kabab is also one of my favourites.In fact any of the kababs you order will be great.
And yes,they also have Chinese items on the menu.God knows why!Its an absolute waste of time,money and resources!
Do stick to the Mughlai and pamper your tummy!

The few other advantages of this particular branch is-
1.All the items are generally available.Some items like the kekuri kabab,Hyderabadi biryani I have found sometimes unavailable in the other outlet nearby towards ajc bose road.
2.The prices are slightly lesser.
3.Service is very fast.
The disadvantage of this branch is that the ambience and decor is a bit inferior to the outlet towards AJC Bose road.

But who cares about ambience and decor when one has such awesome food to indulge in.For me Arsalan serves the best biryani n kababs in town and this outlet is the best option.

As I mentioned earlier the ambiance is decent (a homely atmosphere is always decent and cannot match a 5star restaurant :) ) with average dining facility.
I visited Hyderabad's various popular restaurants to have a taste of the true Hyderabadi Biriyani but those resaturants could'nt help me forget Arsalan,Park Circus,Kolkata
For school and college students with limited pocket money(precisely BIRIYANI lovers)hurry up and visit the place if you havn't done it yet.

I have been longing to visit this joint for a long time.And managed to pay a visit on my birthday.Well i am really impressed after having their food.Needless to say the delicious food made my birthday even more special.
I won't go into details like the location and ambiance of this joint. Because there is nothing extra/special to contribute.Location at 7-point Park Circus crossing is a no-brainer for people of Kolkata. Ambiance in a typical Mughlai joint is run of the mill.The ground floor arrangement is chaos at its best, wherein people are not bothered even to share tables with strangers.They come here to enjoy the food.Nothing else matters.For people who want a little privacy,less noisy atmosphere and cannot survive without an AC, then the first floor section is meant for them.
Now coming to the food.I tried the mutton special biriyani. This dish comprises of 2 large pieces of mutton,1 egg and loads of basmati rice.Enough for 2 people.I have no qualms in admitting that this happens to be one of the best biriyani i have ever had.I will not go into comparisons between different restaurants serving Biriyani in Kolkata. But in my honest opinion Arsalan and Alibaba will take the top honours.
Mutton pasinda and chicken tikka butter masala are the side-dishes that i had ordered.Both comprised of rich gravy along with boneless pieces of meat.However some people might complain about the dishes being very spicy and oily.Some might complain about being salty too.But i found them to be quite appropriate for my taste.
Amongst the bread items roomali roti and butter nan was pretty decent and soft.
Overall a very satisfying experience.Found the food to be delectable and rightly priced.No wonder this joint is crowded throughout the day and expanding rapidly all over the city,Too bad they do not have an outlet at Prince Anwar Shah Road.Are the owners listening? :)

2013-09-11 01:48:12
Chakrabarty
550548
5.0
Yes this is insane! To be specific, their biriyani is!

This restaurant is very easy to locate, just at the famous Park Circus junction. I won't disagree if someone argues that it's not a proper restaurant. It isn't technically. The ground floor is a hot non-AC dining area, where you'd probably have to share table with others. The first floor AC room is small and congested. There's nothing to mention about decor or ambiance. And whichever time I reach there, I see at least 20 people waiting outside (yeah they all know why they are taking the trouble, and that's really worth it). So, you have to wait for sometime before you get your seat. 

After ilish-vs-chingri and east engal-vs-mohan bagan, they next big fight bongs always cherish is the who-serves-the-best-biriyani-in-city. Arsalan, Sheeraz and some other big names have their own huge fan following. While the debate is never conclusive, this place has always been my personal favorite. And I'm sure many others would agree if I say that they serve the best biriyani in the city (and, arguably, in the whole country, after tasting biriyanis from famous restaurants in Hydrabad, Delhi and other cities). 

My all time favorite is Arsalan Special Murgh Biriyani and Mutton Stew. This combo is just out of the world! Takes you to an age of Mughal nawabs, vibrant and dark histories and mysteries. The thin long rices in bright white and yellow, white-ish brown chicken pieces and the smoke coming out of it with a thick aroma, the bowl of dark brown gravy with tender mutton pieces...you have to taste it to understand and feel it. 

You can go with any kebabs to start with, be it tangry kebab, arsalan kebab, malai kebab, hariyali kebab or any random kebab on their menu, you'll not regret it. Same goes for most of the non-veg gravies. I'm not so confident with fish items, they are not known for them. I'll strongly discourage any veg items (sorry, but this is not a good place for pure vegetarians). And don't spoil your time by ordering Chinese, try to stick to Mughlai! Perhaps, it will be wise to refrain from ordering rotis and parathas as well, and let biriyani rule. 

They don't have wide variety in deserts, but I always order firni and soft drinks to complement my biriyani and kebabs.

2013-08-24 03:01:12
Diptanjan Chakraborty
1109853
4.5
I have a bad reputation that i roam across India to taste different types of cuisine . Biriyani is something i love to the core, three types of biriyani's i've tasted till date , Lucknowi, Hyderabadi and The rest (like the Kolkatan ) . But trust me on this note , this one  attracts me the most. A perfect blend of spices, saffron , light, non sticky biriyani  with properly tendered chicken or mutton accompanied by Soft boiled potato covered in biriyani essence  makes it the No. 1 joint to have Briyani in Kolkata. I personally prefer the park circus one because according to them they are having the best group of cooks here . 

SEATING AND SERVICE  :

1.  Downstairs its non air conditioned and you have to share your table with others in case its over crowded . Food tastes the same, but the price of the biriyani and other items are less . somewhere around 10-20 bucks . 

2. If you are bringing your family , there is a staircase on the right side which will lead you to the air conditioned portion of the restaurant which is at first floor . Same food quality with a better ambiance and service . But somehow I find the floor manager bit rude at times and always coming to you and asking whether you are ready to order or not . at times he will indicate passively by asking " do u need anything else? should i make the bill? " . But I can understand that its not his fault but the rush .

FOOD : 
I will recommend 3-4 items, which is a must must try once you step into this place . 
1. Biriyani (be it chicken or mutton ) 
2. Chicken Reshmi Butter Masala   -- white non spicy gravy on a sweeter side with tendered reshmi kababs , 6 pieces . enough for 2 .
3 . Chicken Tikka Kabab--- Very nice Kababs , but you cannot rate it 10 out of 10 .
4. Chicken Tikka Butter Masala --- Same 6 pieces like reshmi butter masala but this time with Tikka Kababs and dark Reddish Spicy Gravy ( goes well with mutton Biriyani )
5 . Firni ( one of the best in entire kolkata / bit overpriced )

PARKING : Infront of the restaurant , beside the sidewalk you can risk parking your car.

POSITION : Situated in the heart of the city . Park Circus 7 Point crossing . Can be reached easily from any direction.

This is heaven for mughlai lovers in kolkata, if somebody is giving a treat the first name which comes to our mind is Arsalan . Cheap , Affordable , *Very *high Quality Food . You will find it the same everytime you visit . 

POINT TO BE NOTED : I had a bad experience on my birthday though. I ordered 10 full reshmi butter masalas and 16 biriyani's and some other side dishes for take away . But reaching home i surprisingly found there were only 3 pieces of chicken in every container . I called them up Immediately and they said sir , please come over and we take your order again and this will be for free, by that time the my mood was completely messed up and i cut the phone . The next time i visited the place i complained , but their answer was are you carrying the previous bill? then we can offer you free food for this time , which i tore long ago.  **** SO if you are having some problem with your food , do tell them and keep the bill . They will take care of that . 

Cheers and ugh ... i wrote too much , you cannot really stop when you start writing about arsalan . BURRRP!

Ahh....Arsalan....Just the name is enough to make my mouth water for an irresistible plate of Biryani ! In my opinion ( and I'm sure many others'), they serve the best Biryani in town. Having studied at Lady Brabourne College, no fest or outing of ours was ever complete without a visit to this place. Even though Park Circus has many places for Mughlai food lovers, this is a standout. And yes, I have tried Shiraz, Zeeshan, Aminia and Rahmania as well !

This particular outlet is almost always overflowing with people and if you are unwilling to share your table with complete strangers, you might have to wait a while to get seated at the upper level (A.C) area. Not that I mind waiting....Cause this is a place where it's all about the Food. Service is fast. And I feel that this kind of ambiance really has a charm of its own....where people seem to take their Biryani pretty seriously !

Coming to the food, there's not much that hasn't been said already ! Both the Chicken and Mutton Biryani are so awesome that many a times I don't even feel the need to have a side dish. And the consistency is remarkable......the Biryani seems to taste exactly the same every time I have it. Simply divine.....And it's kind of addictive ! Your first visit here will never be your last....you can count on that.

Personally, I never found the Biryani to be too oily.....but then, that's just my view. Weight watchers may beg to differ....but to me, when the food is that good, I couldn't care less. Pricing is moderate and doesn't pinch the pocket much, even for a college student. I just couldn't give this place any less than 5 stars. Yes, it may not be perfect in every sphere, but it definitely is a Paradise for Biryani lovers....in every way possible ! :)

2013-08-19 17:06:01
Debdutta Ghosh
1067318
4.5
As everyone here would know, Arsalan is a chain of restaurants known for their exotic Biryanis. The restaurant is located in very accessible area of Park Circus 7 Point Crossing, just next to Jugal's sweets. The restaurant is very small in size and one may find it overcrowded as hell during festive seasons still the service is fast enough and patience for waiting pays off at the end while having the food.

When we talk about the food, any kind of Biryani say Chicken or Mutton will leave you licking your finger. Other than that all kinds of Indian traditional food items are available which are also at par with the Biryani. Fish and Prawn items are also available in the restaurant. Quantity of the food in both take away and dine-in is overwhelming. Prices of items are on the higher side but I personally wont mind paying more to have such tasty food.

Talking of the restaurant's looks and aesthetics, the restaurant has two floors, the ground floor is a non-A/C and first floor is Air Conditioned. The ground floor is very poorly managed with very improper utilization of space, not decorated well and  a filthy toilet to increase your annoyance. The first floor is however slightly better than ground floor but on weekdays or festive seasons if you are able to manage a seat there, consider yourself a lottery winner.

In my opinion, the restaurant seriously needs some renovation and efficient space management to keep up to par with other restaurants in neighboring locations. Considering the adjacent location Park Street, many foreigners would pay a visit to this restaurant but with such poor ambiance one would prefer a take away than a dine-in.

Arsalan is one of the most popular and coverted Biriyani joints in Kolkata. Although to do justice to that tag - they serve very consistent food over time. 

Personally - the highlight is their biriyani. Very lightly done and does not leave an after-taste of dalda. Arsalan Special kebab is a mix of sorts - "hotch-potch" if you can relate to it - it is chicken kebabs coated with cheese. I found rather a mix of strong tastes leading no-where.

Apart from that located very well centrally - service is good , always crowded. Supervised parking available in the lane around - it does get crowded very soon.

If you can't find Arsalan, Park Circus, then you need an appointment with the eye doctor...just kidding. You are at the park circus seven point crossing then you are at Arsalan.

Ambiance is good but the place is overcrowded always. Service (Rating - 2):
As I said if a restaurant gets overcrowded and you have not enough staff then service gets a little compromised. The waiters are very polite and helpful but when they have a rush you will sometimes feel a bit neglected. The worst part of the rush is the waiting time for your food to arrive to you and if you are hungry enough to eat a horse...!!!

Food (Rating - 4):
The food is the most important thing that makes me visit a restaurant over and over again and Arsalan serves really good food. Specially the North Indian dishes and the most renowned dish of Arsalan...BIRYANI...and its YUMMY...!!! The other dishes such as chinese, etc. are not what I consider authentic chinese as many restaurants in Calcutta offer but they are also good.

Price (Rating - 5):
The prices are excellent and very soothing to your pocket. The quantity of the food compared to the pricing is quite decent and filling. You will be happy to eat the food and also happy to pay the bill.

2013-08-13 12:01:46
Anurag Paul
138193
4.5
We have known Hyderabad as the paradise for the Biriyani Lovers, but guess that myth doesn't stand anymore. The Biriyani Joints in Delhi and Lucknow boast of their rich culture in Biriyani which ages older than the Hyderabadi Biriyani.

Not a new but definitely one of the big players in the game is the Kolkata Biriyani which is known for it's subtle taste and variation to the Awadhi biriyani... which has resulted a fame of its own. And to try this whats better than the ultimate destination - 'Arsalan, Park Cirucs'

I must admit, though this joint is famed to be the best Biriyani joint in the City, but the first impression wasn't so attractive and welcoming. People fighting over to get a seat at 3pm on Sunday afternoon in rain, is a pretty common scene here. The restaurant is very conveniently located at Parck Circus 7 point crossing and is difficult to miss.  The restaurant is decent in Size, but definitely small to accommodate the huge parade of Biriyani Lovers that raids this restaurant every day. 

They have two sections, the ground floor housed non-ac section, while the above is A/c section. Depending on that there is small price differences in both the sections. There is huge crowd always in this place, so don't expect much of an ambience. The place is packed with people and noisy which pretty much justifies that the only language this restro speaks of is 'FOOD'.

Now we come to the food quality. I have not tried much of Kolkata biriyani joints as I never lived here. Notable is I tried Aminia once and it was good. Arsalan is definitely better by far. Some people still say that Shiraz Golden Restaurant still serves the best Biriyani in town, but since I haven't tried it once, I'll go with Arsalan, all the time. 

The Biriyani is extremely tasty, but a bit high on oil. We ordered Mutton Spl Biriyani, Chicken Biriyani, Chicken Lahori and  Hariyali Kebab. The Kebab was nice, but I have eaten better kebabs. Chicken Lahori was really good. It seemed very spicy, but the taste was very subtle and you don't burn down your tongue at all. The difference between the normal and Spl biriyani is the quantity, but not the quality. The mutton we very well cooked, almost to perfection as u say, as u would like your mutton to be. The traditional Kolkata Biriyani, with a popato piece and an egg. I loved it and will definitely want to go again.

So I'll just list down the pros and cons of Arsalan, which I felt might be helpful.

Pros:
1. Extremely tasty Biriyani, probably the best in town.
2. Well on price and Budget
3. Centrally located in the city.

Cons:
1. Very crampy place, huge crowd on weekends and festive seasons.
2. Don't expect Privacy or silent dinner, this place is like a busy train station.
3. Biriyani high on oil, so weight conscious people can keep away.

If you want to enjoy their Biriyani, have a takeaway parcel which is available much easier and you can have it in peace. But if you are a Biriyani Lover, you will absorb yourself in the atmosphere of the rush and make yourself comfortable for an amazing Biriyani feast. Enjoy the food!!!

2013-07-22 19:33:22
Mukulita Ganguly
207896
4.0
Park Circus, which can also be rightfully called the biriyani lover‚Äôs paradise, harbours the largest number of Mughlai restaurants in Kolkata, with the most important and debatable one being Arsalan. The unrelenting traffic of the utterly chaotic 7 point leads you to this infamous hub for biryani.

Arsalan may not score well in terms of ambiance, service or the health quotient of the biryani, but I still heart this place for a plethora of reasons (the heavenly taste of the food, some very fond memories with this place and many more).

The ground floor section hosts a swarm of flies along with the irresistible aroma of the super oily food and the first floor's A.C. section is cramped and crowded all the time dotted with some very reluctant servers.

Now, the aforementioned flaws are of little significance to the loyal customers who swear by their biriyani. As I am not too health conscious when it comes to eating, the flavoursome mutton biryani with the huge, tender piece of mutton along with the delectable boiled potato is my personal favourite. On the other hand, the soft and chewy lachha paratha makes a killer combo with any mutton or chicken side dish. Lastly, a plate of kesar flavoured firni is the best dessert to end your meal with.

Overall, this is a place for hardcore foodies who won't mind the extra bit of oil and spices once in a while!

P.S: Weight watchers stay away!

##

2013-07-07 11:09:56
Sanjana Bhattacharyya
235009
3.5
It is part of the triad of Biriyani Mecca of Kolkata: Arsalan-Shiraz-Aminia. Patrons fight over which is the best, but I think Arsalan's a strong contender for the title of 'Best Biriyani Place in Kolkata'.

The biriyani here is really good; it is not too oily, despite a subtle hint of dalda prevailing. I personally have no particular qualms about chomping down dalda-slathered biriyani, but Arsalan does a good job of camouflaging the shortening's fatty flavour in aromatic spices. They certainly don't skimp on the pieces of mutton in the Biriyani, but when I had the chicken Biriyani, I found the piece of meat disappointingly skinny. On the very few occasions 


The kebabs are beautiful to taste; the spice coat, the amount of char, the texture of the chicken are all near perfect. I prefer the Reshmi kebabs, but I have been reliably informed that the Kakori and Hariyali kebabs are 'absolutely sinful'.

The side dishes, however, I cannot rave about. They repeatedly fail to impress me. Most of the time, the creamy 'butter' dishes are too sweet for my liking. I prefer Only Alibaba's slightly tangy taste. The pieces of chicken (I never order mutton sides, so I can't vouch for that), though not exactly tough, are not as succulent as I like them to be. The gravy almost always has a curdled look that I find particularly unappetizing. 

As for the service, it's not up to the mark. The waiters have the same couldn't-care-less attitude that I have seen in so many mid- to low-range restaurants in Kolkata. On more than one occasion, we had to ask for a glass of water after getting our seats, forget about refills. For every dish we ordered, for the glass of water, for the refills, even for the bill there was a tedious wait. In fact, the last time I went there with a friend, it was just noon, the restaurant was not even half-filled, and the waiter asked us to sit at a table side by side, cramped together, instead of sitting comfortably facing each other. I have no idea how this could help them or anyone, but it was certainly a very uncomfortable lunch with both of us trying hard to fit the dishes on a table that's meant to serve one person on each side.

2013-07-05 10:37:19
Somnath Basu
676598
3.5
This Arsalan outlet is possibly the one that serves the best food among the four or five in the city. It is perpetually crowded, which makes entry a problem, but for those who like Mughlai food, it might be worth the wait.

Reams have been written about Arsalan's biriyani, with fierce debates about whether it is the best biriyani in the city, or whether some other restaurant makes better biriyani. I will pass over that and merely say that the biriyani here is certainly very good.

There are other items on the menu that are worthy of attention. The Arsalan Special Kebab, which is coated in melted cheese, is a hybrid dish, but hard to resist. Not too much has been said about the very good Tandoori Rotis and Lachcha Parathas available here. Most of the mutton dishes are good, and the Arsalan Murgh Makhani deserves special mention among the chicken dishes.

The service has been variable. I agree with many reviewers who say that the waiters have been rude.  I must also say that I have always been served by polite and friendly waiters every time I have been there (till date). Dishes that are pre-prepared, like the biriyani, arrive quickly, but other dishes take time.

In many Mughlai restaurants, individuals or groups of up to three people do share tables with other individuals or groups - it is traditional, but usually does not happen in the air-conditioned section of the restaurant.

Overall, a good place to go to for Mughlai food, provided you are willing to brave the crowds.

##

2013-03-18 17:30:27
Bhavesh Bhatia
199538
4.5
Residing at the East of Kolkata, one gets ample access to the famous Mughlai and Chinese food joints of the city, be it 'Shiraz', 'Zeeshan' or 'Beijing'. So when it came to reviewing 'Arsalan' Restaurant's main branch, I gladly welcomed it. Now, why did I mention the other three eateries if I am to review the fourth one? The answer is pretty simple. Since 2002 when Arsalan started operatiing, it has axed the popularity of the former three. Arsalan serves Mughlai as well as Chinese delicacies but it is best known for its penchant in Mughlai dishes.
I went there to find out exactly why people preferred it to the others.

Situated at one of the busiest crossings of Kolkata, the Park Circus seven point crossing; Arsalan can be surely tagged as one of the landmarks here. The first thing to catch the eye is its name and the abundant space inside. It has nothing to do with the interior decor. After I had a chat with the owner I got to know that more than anything they are concerned about the quality of food they serve. According to him, people go to a restaurant for eating not to see its decor. If the food is good they will visit it again. Still, if someone prefers good interiors and food with equal interest they should seat themselves on the first floor of this joint.

Mughlai food is known for its richness. It is famous for the exotic use of spices, dry fruits and nuts with style and splendor. Here, the dishes start from a mere 80 bucks and can shoot up to as much as 7000! The dishes include Biriyani, Kababs, Tandoori, Noodles, Soup and much more, but the dish which I liked most was their 'Kakori Kabab'. Made with mince meat, it's so tender that it simply melts in your mouth, flavored with god knows what spices! Who cares when you are eating such delicious food!

Arsalan opens at 12 PM and serves customers till 1.30 AM on normal days. During festivities it remains open till 4 AM.I have personally never seen the entrance of this food joint deserted whenever I have walked past the place. 

Am I being biased that I didn't find anything to negate? Well, there are a few negative points as well. If you plan to visit this place, you better travel by public transport because finding parking is near impossible. Get something to pass your time in the queue; it may take as long as 45 minutes to get your order served!

But I think the people of Kolkata are still crazy foodies or else this food joint wouldn't have run this well for 11 years with its 4 branches (one situated at Mumbai)!

If its Biriyani that you want in Kolkata, then its gotta be Arsalan. the best place for biriyani and kebabs in Kol.

Quality: has been top class. All the items are well cooked and nothing really to say about the taste, its bang on.

Price: Pretty competitive, recently prices have increased, yet you wouldnt mind spending that extra buck for the quality of food that you get.

Try their rolls, im a big fan of those. If its mughlai, then its Arsalan.

======== Update as on 6 DEC 2016 ========

Mutton Biryani: Obviously the signature dish, extremely well cooked and flavoured. The mutton piece was decent and well cooked (although my favourite would be the mutton piece of Dada Boudi's biryani). The potato and rice was awesome. This dish is definitely and without any doubt one of the best biryanis in Kolkata. Do not miss this. I can just wonder how awesome the special biryani will be. Will try it next time.

Chicken Achari Masala: Super delicious gravy, that tangy-spicy taste is really unique and the chicken pieces were well cooked and soft. Enjoyed it very much with the mutton biryani but this dish will go well with any roti.

Chicken Hariyali Masala: Again a lovely dish. The gravy looks lovely and tastes very good. But it is painful for me to say that the chicken pieces were very hard and felt like they were a week old. Totally opposite of the achari dish.

I would highly recommend this place to everyone. If you are in Kolkata and haven't visited this place then you haven't experienced Kolkata yet.

The menu card is long. My reco to friends is that do not waste ur precious time , energy & imagination - just order Arsalan special mutton Biryani with Mutton kosha, ishtew & chhamp as side dishes. This word of wisdom comes after multiple visits - These r the gems - rest are good but these r the best in town. 

Kolkata Biryani is a version of Lucknow Dum Biryani in which the meat & the rice is slow cooked, (sometimes with milk instead of water). You get a piece of half a potato & a boiled egg as a part of The Biryani. 

The rice strands of the biryani melt in the mouth, burst with flavors of the spices & the meat & most importantly the rice strands do not stick to each other. The meat flavors are unique due to the spices used & slow cooking tenderizes the meat to an extent that it melts in the mouth. The potato is cooked with the biryani - so the flavors enter it & the egg is unnecessary but interesting & fun to munch on.

History of Kolkata Biryani: When Wazid Ali Shah, the Nawab of Lucknow was deported by the British to Kolkata, he got with an entourage of cooks, nautch girls & many more things. What has predominantly remained intact after few centuries, is the cuisine that those cooks introduced to this part of the country (with some modifications). 

Regarding the meat dishes, all of them are unique, sip water / cola between the two dishes - u will distinctly understand the differences. The meats are cooked in the gravy & hence are full of flavors. They are surely oily & not for the faint hearted. 

In case u r not sure how ur tummy's goin to behave the next day, just pop in pudin haras:)

To end it all - Your taste buddies (buds) will thank u for taking them to Arsalan - U just have to do a bit more of cardio next week to burn those extra calories:)

We went there on last Sunday [26Jun'11]. This was the first time we visited this particular branch of Arsalan. We had to wait for 20--30 minutes. The outside was quiet and waiting crowd was good. Inside ambiance is very much homely. The food quality and taste is VERY GOOD!!!! We must say that this is the best Biriyani we had in this level of restaurants. Other dishes were equally well. Every item is well cooked, easy to digest, no stomach problem. The staff are well behaved and professional. Price is reasonable [M-Biriyani Rs.100/-, M-Pasinda Rs. 140/-, Half-Ch-Tandoori Rs.120/- on date].
Some items like Hyderabadi Biriyani which they stopped making is still there in the menu. I think they should consider a smaller menu which they can deliver.
Good place [just this Circus Avenue Branch of Arsalan] to visit often.

2011-02-23 12:02:27
Atmadeep Sengupta

3.0
Arsalan undoubtedly is one of the best Mughlai restaurants in Kolkata. The restaurant has a charm of its own.  The very essence of Arsalan lies in the fact that the mughal cuisines created by them has more of Nawabi elements of Bengal which is quiet different than the Awadhi or Hyderabadi style of cooking. The sumptuous biriyani's helped with a potato and egg makes it a fulfilling gastronomical extravaganza. The kebabs and the ghosht (mutton) are the best. A special kebab made by cheese and chicken ( Arsalan Special Kebab) is sure to take your breath away. Even in the din and the hustle of the crowd (which is a natural consequence  to their ever increasing popularity) it is one of the places to have mughlai in Kolkata.
